140#define STBTT_iceil(x) ((int)ImCeil(x))
141#define STBTT_STATIC
142#define STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION
143#else
144#define STBTT_DEF extern
145#endif

356//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
357// [SECTION] ImDrawList
358//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
359
360ImDrawListSharedData::ImDrawListSharedData()
361{
362 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
363 for (int i = 0; i < IM_ARRAYSIZE(ArcFastVtx); i++)
364 {
365 const float a = ((float)i * 2 * IM_PI) / (float)IM_ARRAYSIZE(ArcFastVtx);
366 ArcFastVtx[i] = ImVec2(ImCos(a), ImSin(a));
367 }
368 ArcFastRadiusCutoff = IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC_R(IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, CircleSegmentMaxError);
369}
370
371void ImDrawListSharedData::SetCircleTessellationMaxError(float max_error)
372{
373 if (CircleSegmentMaxError == max_error)
374 return;
375
376 IM_ASSERT(max_error > 0.0f);
377 CircleSegmentMaxError = max_error;
378 for (int i = 0; i < IM_ARRAYSIZE(CircleSegmentCounts); i++)
379 {
380 const float radius = (float)i;
381 CircleSegmentCounts[i] = (ImU8)((i > 0) ? IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC(radius, CircleSegmentMaxError) : IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX);
382 }
383 ArcFastRadiusCutoff = IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC_R(IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, CircleSegmentMaxError);
384}
385
386// Initialize before use in a new frame. We always have a command ready in the buffer.
387void ImDrawList::_ResetForNewFrame()
388{
389 // Verify that the ImDrawCmd fields we want to memcmp() are contiguous in memory.
390 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(ImDrawCmd, ClipRect) == 0);
391 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(ImDrawCmd, TextureId) == sizeof(ImVec4));
392 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(offsetof(ImDrawCmd, VtxOffset) == sizeof(ImVec4) + sizeof(ImTextureID));
393 if (_Splitter._Count > 1)
394 _Splitter.Merge(this);
395
396 CmdBuffer.resize(0);
397 IdxBuffer.resize(0);
398 VtxBuffer.resize(0);
399 Flags = _Data->InitialFlags;
400 memset(&_CmdHeader, 0, sizeof(_CmdHeader));
401 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
402 _VtxWritePtr = NULL;
403 _IdxWritePtr = NULL;
404 _ClipRectStack.resize(0);
405 _TextureIdStack.resize(0);
406 _Path.resize(0);
407 _Splitter.Clear();
408 CmdBuffer.push_back(ImDrawCmd());
409 _FringeScale = 1.0f;
410}
411
412void ImDrawList::_ClearFreeMemory()
413{
414 CmdBuffer.clear();
415 IdxBuffer.clear();
416 VtxBuffer.clear();
417 Flags = ImDrawListFlags_None;
418 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
419 _VtxWritePtr = NULL;
420 _IdxWritePtr = NULL;
421 _ClipRectStack.clear();
422 _TextureIdStack.clear();
423 _Path.clear();
424 _Splitter.ClearFreeMemory();
425}
426
427ImDrawList* ImDrawList::CloneOutput() const
428{
429 ImDrawList* dst = IM_NEW(ImDrawList(_Data));
430 dst->CmdBuffer = CmdBuffer;
431 dst->IdxBuffer = IdxBuffer;
432 dst->VtxBuffer = VtxBuffer;
433 dst->Flags = Flags;
434 return dst;
435}
436
437void ImDrawList::AddDrawCmd()
438{
439 ImDrawCmd draw_cmd;
440 draw_cmd.ClipRect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect; // Same as calling ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy()
441 draw_cmd.TextureId = _CmdHeader.TextureId;
442 draw_cmd.VtxOffset = _CmdHeader.VtxOffset;
443 draw_cmd.IdxOffset = IdxBuffer.Size;
444
445 IM_ASSERT(draw_cmd.ClipRect.x <= draw_cmd.ClipRect.z && draw_cmd.ClipRect.y <= draw_cmd.ClipRect.w);
446 CmdBuffer.push_back(draw_cmd);
447}
448
449// Pop trailing draw command (used before merging or presenting to user)
450// Note that this leaves the ImDrawList in a state unfit for further commands, as most code assume that CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback == NULL
451void ImDrawList::_PopUnusedDrawCmd()
452{
453 while (CmdBuffer.Size > 0)
454 {
455 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
456 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 || curr_cmd->UserCallback != NULL)
457 return;// break;
458 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
459 }
460}
461
462void ImDrawList::AddCallback(ImDrawCallback callback, void* callback_data)
463{
464 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
465 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
466 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
467 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0)
468 {
469 AddDrawCmd();
470 curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
471 }
472 curr_cmd->UserCallback = callback;
473 curr_cmd->UserCallbackData = callback_data;
474
475 AddDrawCmd(); // Force a new command after us (see comment below)
476}
477
478// Compare ClipRect, TextureId and VtxOffset with a single memcmp()
479#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize (offsetof(ImDrawCmd, VtxOffset) + sizeof(unsigned int))
480#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(CMD_LHS, CMD_RHS) (memcmp(CMD_LHS, CMD_RHS, ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize)) // Compare ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
481#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(CMD_DST, CMD_SRC) (memcpy(CMD_DST, CMD_SRC, ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize)) // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
482#define ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(CMD_0, CMD_1) (CMD_0->IdxOffset + CMD_0->ElemCount == CMD_1->IdxOffset)
483
484// Try to merge two last draw commands
485void ImDrawList::_TryMergeDrawCmds()
486{
487 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
488 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
489 ImDrawCmd* prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
490 if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
491 {
492 prev_cmd->ElemCount += curr_cmd->ElemCount;
493 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
494 }
495}
496
497// Our scheme may appears a bit unusual, basically we want the most-common calls AddLine AddRect etc. to not have to perform any check so we always have a command ready in the stack.
498// The cost of figuring out if a new command has to be added or if we can merge is paid in those Update** functions only.
499void ImDrawList::_OnChangedClipRect()
500{
501 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
502 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
503 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
504 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 && memcmp(&curr_cmd->ClipRect, &_CmdHeader.ClipRect, sizeof(ImVec4)) != 0)
505 {
506 AddDrawCmd();
507 return;
508 }
509 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
510
511 // Try to merge with previous command if it matches, else use current command
512 ImDrawCmd* prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
513 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0 && CmdBuffer.Size > 1 && ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(&_CmdHeader, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
514 {
515 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
516 return;
517 }
518
519 curr_cmd->ClipRect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
520}
521
522void ImDrawList::_OnChangedTextureID()
523{
524 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
525 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
526 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
527 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 && curr_cmd->TextureId != _CmdHeader.TextureId)
528 {
529 AddDrawCmd();
530 return;
531 }
532 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
533
534 // Try to merge with previous command if it matches, else use current command
535 ImDrawCmd* prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
536 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0 && CmdBuffer.Size > 1 && ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(&_CmdHeader, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
537 {
538 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
539 return;
540 }
541
542 curr_cmd->TextureId = _CmdHeader.TextureId;
543}
544
545void ImDrawList::_OnChangedVtxOffset()
546{
547 // We don't need to compare curr_cmd->VtxOffset != _CmdHeader.VtxOffset because we know it'll be different at the time we call this.
548 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
549 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
550 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
551 //IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->VtxOffset != _CmdHeader.VtxOffset); // See #3349
552 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0)
553 {
554 AddDrawCmd();
555 return;
556 }
557 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
558 curr_cmd->VtxOffset = _CmdHeader.VtxOffset;
559}
560
561int ImDrawList::_CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(float radius) const
562{
563 // Automatic segment count
564 const int radius_idx = (int)(radius + 0.999999f); // ceil to never reduce accuracy
565 if (radius_idx >= 0 && radius_idx < IM_ARRAYSIZE(_Data->CircleSegmentCounts))
566 return _Data->CircleSegmentCounts[radius_idx]; // Use cached value
567 else
568 return IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC(radius, _Data->CircleSegmentMaxError);
569}
570
571// Render-level scissoring. This is passed down to your render function but not used for CPU-side coarse clipping. Prefer using higher-level ImGui::PushClipRect() to affect logic (hit-testing and widget culling)
572void ImDrawList::PushClipRect(const ImVec2& cr_min, const ImVec2& cr_max, bool intersect_with_current_clip_rect)
573{
574 ImVec4 cr(cr_min.x, cr_min.y, cr_max.x, cr_max.y);
575 if (intersect_with_current_clip_rect)
576 {
577 ImVec4 current = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
578 if (cr.x < current.x) cr.x = current.x;
579 if (cr.y < current.y) cr.y = current.y;
580 if (cr.z > current.z) cr.z = current.z;
581 if (cr.w > current.w) cr.w = current.w;
582 }
583 cr.z = ImMax(cr.x, cr.z);
584 cr.w = ImMax(cr.y, cr.w);
585
586 _ClipRectStack.push_back(cr);
587 _CmdHeader.ClipRect = cr;
588 _OnChangedClipRect();
589}
590
591void ImDrawList::PushClipRectFullScreen()
592{
593 PushClipRect(ImVec2(_Data->ClipRectFullscreen.x, _Data->ClipRectFullscreen.y), ImVec2(_Data->ClipRectFullscreen.z, _Data->ClipRectFullscreen.w));
594}
595
596void ImDrawList::PopClipRect()
597{
598 _ClipRectStack.pop_back();
599 _CmdHeader.ClipRect = (_ClipRectStack.Size == 0) ? _Data->ClipRectFullscreen : _ClipRectStack.Data[_ClipRectStack.Size - 1];
600 _OnChangedClipRect();
601}
602
603void ImDrawList::PushTextureID(ImTextureID texture_id)
604{
605 _TextureIdStack.push_back(texture_id);
606 _CmdHeader.TextureId = texture_id;
607 _OnChangedTextureID();
608}
609
610void ImDrawList::PopTextureID()
611{
612 _TextureIdStack.pop_back();
613 _CmdHeader.TextureId = (_TextureIdStack.Size == 0) ? (ImTextureID)NULL : _TextureIdStack.Data[_TextureIdStack.Size - 1];
614 _OnChangedTextureID();
615}
616
617// Reserve space for a number of vertices and indices.
618// You must finish filling your reserved data before calling PrimReserve() again, as it may reallocate or
619// submit the intermediate results. PrimUnreserve() can be used to release unused allocations.
620void ImDrawList::PrimReserve(int idx_count, int vtx_count)
621{
622 // Large mesh support (when enabled)
623 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(idx_count >= 0 && vtx_count >= 0);
624 if (sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2 && (_VtxCurrentIdx + vtx_count >= (1 << 16)) && (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AllowVtxOffset))
625 {
626 // FIXME: In theory we should be testing that vtx_count <64k here.
627 // In practice, RenderText() relies on reserving ahead for a worst case scenario so it is currently useful for us
628 // to not make that check until we rework the text functions to handle clipping and large horizontal lines better.
629 _CmdHeader.VtxOffset = VtxBuffer.Size;
630 _OnChangedVtxOffset();
631 }
632
633 ImDrawCmd* draw_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
634 draw_cmd->ElemCount += idx_count;
635
636 int vtx_buffer_old_size = VtxBuffer.Size;
637 VtxBuffer.resize(vtx_buffer_old_size + vtx_count);
638 _VtxWritePtr = VtxBuffer.Data + vtx_buffer_old_size;
639
640 int idx_buffer_old_size = IdxBuffer.Size;
641 IdxBuffer.resize(idx_buffer_old_size + idx_count);
642 _IdxWritePtr = IdxBuffer.Data + idx_buffer_old_size;
643}
644
645// Release the number of reserved vertices/indices from the end of the last reservation made with PrimReserve().
646void ImDrawList::PrimUnreserve(int idx_count, int vtx_count)
647{
648 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(idx_count >= 0 && vtx_count >= 0);
649
650 ImDrawCmd* draw_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
651 draw_cmd->ElemCount -= idx_count;
652 VtxBuffer.shrink(VtxBuffer.Size - vtx_count);
653 IdxBuffer.shrink(IdxBuffer.Size - idx_count);
654}
655
656// Fully unrolled with inline call to keep our debug builds decently fast.
657void ImDrawList::PrimRect(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& c, ImU32 col)
658{
659 ImVec2 b(c.x, a.y), d(a.x, c.y), uv(_Data->TexUvWhitePixel);
660 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
661 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2);
662 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+3);
663 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
664 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
665 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
666 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
667 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
668 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
669 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
670}
671
672void ImDrawList::PrimRectUV(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& c, const ImVec2& uv_a, const ImVec2& uv_c, ImU32 col)
673{
674 ImVec2 b(c.x, a.y), d(a.x, c.y), uv_b(uv_c.x, uv_a.y), uv_d(uv_a.x, uv_c.y);
675 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
676 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2);
677 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+3);
678 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv_a; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
679 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv_b; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
680 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv_c; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
681 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv_d; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
682 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
683 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
684 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
685}
686
687void ImDrawList::PrimQuadUV(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& b, const ImVec2& c, const ImVec2& d, const ImVec2& uv_a, const ImVec2& uv_b, const ImVec2& uv_c, const ImVec2& uv_d, ImU32 col)
688{
689 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
690 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2);
691 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+3);
692 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv_a; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
693 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv_b; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
694 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv_c; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
695 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv_d; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
696 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
697 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
698 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
699}
700
701// On AddPolyline() and AddConvexPolyFilled() we intentionally avoid using ImVec2 and superfluous function calls to optimize debug/non-inlined builds.
702// - Those macros expects l-values and need to be used as their own statement.
703// - Those macros are intentionally not surrounded by the 'do {} while (0)' idiom because even that translates to runtime with debug compilers.
704#define IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(VX,VY) { float d2 = VX*VX + VY*VY; if (d2 > 0.0f) { float inv_len = ImRsqrt(d2); VX *= inv_len; VY *= inv_len; } } (void)0
705#define IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2 100.0f // 500.0f (see #4053, #3366)
706#define IM_FIXNORMAL2F(VX,VY) { float d2 = VX*VX + VY*VY; if (d2 > 0.000001f) { float inv_len2 = 1.0f / d2; if (inv_len2 > IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2) inv_len2 = IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2; VX *= inv_len2; VY *= inv_len2; } } (void)0
707
708// TODO: Thickness anti-aliased lines cap are missing their AA fringe.
709// We avoid using the ImVec2 math operators here to reduce cost to a minimum for debug/non-inlined builds.
710void ImDrawList::AddPolyline(const ImVec2* points, const int points_count, ImU32 col, ImDrawFlags flags, float thickness)
711{
712 if (points_count < 2 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
713 return;
714
715 const bool closed = (flags & ImDrawFlags_Closed) != 0;
716 const ImVec2 opaque_uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
717 const int count = closed ? points_count : points_count - 1; // The number of line segments we need to draw
718 const bool thick_line = (thickness > _FringeScale);
719
720 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLines)
721 {
722 // Anti-aliased stroke
723 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
724 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
725
726 // Thicknesses <1.0 should behave like thickness 1.0
727 thickness = ImMax(thickness, 1.0f);
728 const int integer_thickness = (int)thickness;
729 const float fractional_thickness = thickness - integer_thickness;
730
731 // Do we want to draw this line using a texture?
732 // - For now, only draw integer-width lines using textures to avoid issues with the way scaling occurs, could be improved.
733 // - If AA_SIZE is not 1.0f we cannot use the texture path.
734 const bool use_texture = (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex) && (integer_thickness < IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX) && (fractional_thickness <= 0.00001f) && (AA_SIZE == 1.0f);
735
736 // We should never hit this, because NewFrame() doesn't set ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex unless ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines is off
737 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(!use_texture || !(_Data->Font->ContainerAtlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines));
738
739 const int idx_count = use_texture ? (count * 6) : (thick_line ? count * 18 : count * 12);
740 const int vtx_count = use_texture ? (points_count * 2) : (thick_line ? points_count * 4 : points_count * 3);
741 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
742
743 // Temporary buffer
744 // The first <points_count> items are normals at each line point, then after that there are either 2 or 4 temp points for each line point
745 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count * ((use_texture || !thick_line) ? 3 : 5));
746 ImVec2* temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
747 ImVec2* temp_points = temp_normals + points_count;
748
749 // Calculate normals (tangents) for each line segment
750 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++)
751 {
752 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1;
753 float dx = points[i2].x - points[i1].x;
754 float dy = points[i2].y - points[i1].y;
755 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
756 temp_normals[i1].x = dy;
757 temp_normals[i1].y = -dx;
758 }
759 if (!closed)
760 temp_normals[points_count - 1] = temp_normals[points_count - 2];
761
762 // If we are drawing a one-pixel-wide line without a texture, or a textured line of any width, we only need 2 or 3 vertices per point
763 if (use_texture || !thick_line)
764 {
765 // [PATH 1] Texture-based lines (thick or non-thick)
766 // [PATH 2] Non texture-based lines (non-thick)
767
768 // The width of the geometry we need to draw - this is essentially <thickness> pixels for the line itself, plus "one pixel" for AA.
769 // - In the texture-based path, we don't use AA_SIZE here because the +1 is tied to the generated texture
770 // (see ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData() function), and so alternate values won't work without changes to that code.
771 // - In the non texture-based paths, we would allow AA_SIZE to potentially be != 1.0f with a patch (e.g. fringe_scale patch to
772 // allow scaling geometry while preserving one-screen-pixel AA fringe).
773 const float half_draw_size = use_texture ? ((thickness * 0.5f) + 1) : AA_SIZE;
774
775 // If line is not closed, the first and last points need to be generated differently as there are no normals to blend
776 if (!closed)
777 {
778 temp_points[0] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * half_draw_size;
779 temp_points[1] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * half_draw_size;
780 temp_points[(points_count-1)*2+0] = points[points_count-1] + temp_normals[points_count-1] * half_draw_size;
781 temp_points[(points_count-1)*2+1] = points[points_count-1] - temp_normals[points_count-1] * half_draw_size;
782 }
783
784 // Generate the indices to form a number of triangles for each line segment, and the vertices for the line edges
785 // This takes points n and n+1 and writes into n+1, with the first point in a closed line being generated from the final one (as n+1 wraps)
786 // FIXME-OPT: Merge the different loops, possibly remove the temporary buffer.
787 unsigned int idx1 = _VtxCurrentIdx; // Vertex index for start of line segment
788 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++) // i1 is the first point of the line segment
789 {
790 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1; // i2 is the second point of the line segment
791 const unsigned int idx2 = ((i1 + 1) == points_count) ? _VtxCurrentIdx : (idx1 + (use_texture ? 2 : 3)); // Vertex index for end of segment
792
793 // Average normals
794 float dm_x = (temp_normals[i1].x + temp_normals[i2].x) * 0.5f;
795 float dm_y = (temp_normals[i1].y + temp_normals[i2].y) * 0.5f;
796 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
797 dm_x *= half_draw_size; // dm_x, dm_y are offset to the outer edge of the AA area
798 dm_y *= half_draw_size;
799
800 // Add temporary vertexes for the outer edges
801 ImVec2* out_vtx = &temp_points[i2 * 2];
802 out_vtx[0].x = points[i2].x + dm_x;
803 out_vtx[0].y = points[i2].y + dm_y;
804 out_vtx[1].x = points[i2].x - dm_x;
805 out_vtx[1].y = points[i2].y - dm_y;
806
807 if (use_texture)
808 {
809 // Add indices for two triangles
810 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); // Right tri
811 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); // Left tri
812 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
813 }
814 else
815 {
816 // Add indexes for four triangles
817 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); // Right tri 1
818 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); // Right tri 2
819 _IdxWritePtr[6] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[7] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[8] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); // Left tri 1
820 _IdxWritePtr[9] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[10] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[11] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); // Left tri 2
821 _IdxWritePtr += 12;
822 }
823
824 idx1 = idx2;
825 }
826
827 // Add vertexes for each point on the line
828 if (use_texture)
829 {
830 // If we're using textures we only need to emit the left/right edge vertices
831 ImVec4 tex_uvs = _Data->TexUvLines[integer_thickness];
832 /*if (fractional_thickness != 0.0f) // Currently always zero when use_texture==false!
833 {
834 const ImVec4 tex_uvs_1 = _Data->TexUvLines[integer_thickness + 1];
835 tex_uvs.x = tex_uvs.x + (tex_uvs_1.x - tex_uvs.x) * fractional_thickness; // inlined ImLerp()
836 tex_uvs.y = tex_uvs.y + (tex_uvs_1.y - tex_uvs.y) * fractional_thickness;
837 tex_uvs.z = tex_uvs.z + (tex_uvs_1.z - tex_uvs.z) * fractional_thickness;
838 tex_uvs.w = tex_uvs.w + (tex_uvs_1.w - tex_uvs.w) * fractional_thickness;
839 }*/
840 ImVec2 tex_uv0(tex_uvs.x, tex_uvs.y);
841 ImVec2 tex_uv1(tex_uvs.z, tex_uvs.w);
842 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
843 {
844 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 0]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = tex_uv0; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Left-side outer edge
845 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 1]; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = tex_uv1; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col; // Right-side outer edge
846 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
847 }
848 }
849 else
850 {
851 // If we're not using a texture, we need the center vertex as well
852 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
853 {
854 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Center of line
855 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 0]; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Left-side outer edge
856 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 1]; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col_trans; // Right-side outer edge
857 _VtxWritePtr += 3;
858 }
859 }
860 }
861 else
862 {
863 // [PATH 2] Non texture-based lines (thick): we need to draw the solid line core and thus require four vertices per point
864 const float half_inner_thickness = (thickness - AA_SIZE) * 0.5f;
865
866 // If line is not closed, the first and last points need to be generated differently as there are no normals to blend
867 if (!closed)
868 {
869 const int points_last = points_count - 1;
870 temp_points[0] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
871 temp_points[1] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness);
872 temp_points[2] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness);
873 temp_points[3] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
874 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 0] = points[points_last] + temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
875 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 1] = points[points_last] + temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness);
876 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 2] = points[points_last] - temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness);
877 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 3] = points[points_last] - temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
878 }
879
880 // Generate the indices to form a number of triangles for each line segment, and the vertices for the line edges
881 // This takes points n and n+1 and writes into n+1, with the first point in a closed line being generated from the final one (as n+1 wraps)
882 // FIXME-OPT: Merge the different loops, possibly remove the temporary buffer.
883 unsigned int idx1 = _VtxCurrentIdx; // Vertex index for start of line segment
884 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++) // i1 is the first point of the line segment
885 {
886 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : (i1 + 1); // i2 is the second point of the line segment
887 const unsigned int idx2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? _VtxCurrentIdx : (idx1 + 4); // Vertex index for end of segment
888
889 // Average normals
890 float dm_x = (temp_normals[i1].x + temp_normals[i2].x) * 0.5f;
891 float dm_y = (temp_normals[i1].y + temp_normals[i2].y) * 0.5f;
892 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
893 float dm_out_x = dm_x * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
894 float dm_out_y = dm_y * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
895 float dm_in_x = dm_x * half_inner_thickness;
896 float dm_in_y = dm_y * half_inner_thickness;
897
898 // Add temporary vertices
899 ImVec2* out_vtx = &temp_points[i2 * 4];
900 out_vtx[0].x = points[i2].x + dm_out_x;
901 out_vtx[0].y = points[i2].y + dm_out_y;
902 out_vtx[1].x = points[i2].x + dm_in_x;
903 out_vtx[1].y = points[i2].y + dm_in_y;
904 out_vtx[2].x = points[i2].x - dm_in_x;
905 out_vtx[2].y = points[i2].y - dm_in_y;
906 out_vtx[3].x = points[i2].x - dm_out_x;
907 out_vtx[3].y = points[i2].y - dm_out_y;
908
909 // Add indexes
910 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2);
911 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
912 _IdxWritePtr[6] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[7] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[8] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0);
913 _IdxWritePtr[9] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[10] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[11] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
914 _IdxWritePtr[12] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[13] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[14] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 3);
915 _IdxWritePtr[15] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 3); _IdxWritePtr[16] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 3); _IdxWritePtr[17] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2);
916 _IdxWritePtr += 18;
917
918 idx1 = idx2;
919 }
920
921 // Add vertices
922 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
923 {
924 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 0]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col_trans;
925 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 1]; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
926 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 2]; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
927 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 3]; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col_trans;
928 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
929 }
930 }
931 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
932 }
933 else
934 {
935 // [PATH 4] Non texture-based, Non anti-aliased lines
936 const int idx_count = count * 6;
937 const int vtx_count = count * 4; // FIXME-OPT: Not sharing edges
938 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
939
940 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++)
941 {
942 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1;
943 const ImVec2& p1 = points[i1];
944 const ImVec2& p2 = points[i2];
945
946 float dx = p2.x - p1.x;
947 float dy = p2.y - p1.y;
948 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
949 dx *= (thickness * 0.5f);
950 dy *= (thickness * 0.5f);
951
952 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = p1.x + dy; _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = p1.y - dx; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
953 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = p2.x + dy; _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = p2.y - dx; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
954 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos.x = p2.x - dy; _VtxWritePtr[2].pos.y = p2.y + dx; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
955 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos.x = p1.x - dy; _VtxWritePtr[3].pos.y = p1.y + dx; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
956 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
957
958 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2);
959 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 3);
960 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
961 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
962 }
963 }
964}
965
966// - We intentionally avoid using ImVec2 and its math operators here to reduce cost to a minimum for debug/non-inlined builds.
967// - Filled shapes must always use clockwise winding order. The anti-aliasing fringe depends on it. Counter-clockwise shapes will have "inward" anti-aliasing.
968void ImDrawList::AddConvexPolyFilled(const ImVec2* points, const int points_count, ImU32 col)
969{
970 if (points_count < 3 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
971 return;
972
973 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
974
975 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedFill)
976 {
977 // Anti-aliased Fill
978 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
979 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
980 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2)*3 + points_count * 6;
981 const int vtx_count = (points_count * 2);
982 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
983
984 // Add indexes for fill
985 unsigned int vtx_inner_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx;
986 unsigned int vtx_outer_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx + 1;
987 for (int i = 2; i < points_count; i++)
988 {
989 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + ((i - 1) << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i << 1));
990 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
991 }
992
993 // Compute normals
994 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count);
995 ImVec2* temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
996 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
997 {
998 const ImVec2& p0 = points[i0];
999 const ImVec2& p1 = points[i1];
1000 float dx = p1.x - p0.x;
1001 float dy = p1.y - p0.y;
1002 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
1003 temp_normals[i0].x = dy;
1004 temp_normals[i0].y = -dx;
1005 }
1006
1007 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
1008 {
1009 // Average normals
1010 const ImVec2& n0 = temp_normals[i0];
1011 const ImVec2& n1 = temp_normals[i1];
1012 float dm_x = (n0.x + n1.x) * 0.5f;
1013 float dm_y = (n0.y + n1.y) * 0.5f;
1014 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
1015 dm_x *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1016 dm_y *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1017
1018 // Add vertices
1019 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = (points[i1].x - dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = (points[i1].y - dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Inner
1020 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = (points[i1].x + dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = (points[i1].y + dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Outer
1021 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
1022
1023 // Add indexes for fringes
1024 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1));
1025 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1));
1026 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
1027 }
1028 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1029 }
1030 else
1031 {
1032 // Non Anti-aliased Fill
1033 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2)*3;
1034 const int vtx_count = points_count;
1035 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1036 for (int i = 0; i < vtx_count; i++)
1037 {
1038 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
1039 _VtxWritePtr++;
1040 }
1041 for (int i = 2; i < points_count; i++)
1042 {
1043 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + i - 1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + i);
1044 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
1045 }
1046 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1047 }
1048}
1049
1050void ImDrawList::_PathArcToFastEx(const ImVec2& center, float radius, int a_min_sample, int a_max_sample, int a_step)
1051{
1052 if (radius < 0.5f)
1053 {
1054 _Path.push_back(center);
1055 return;
1056 }
1057
1058 // Calculate arc auto segment step size
1059 if (a_step <= 0)
1060 a_step = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(radius);
1061
1062 // Make sure we never do steps larger than one quarter of the circle
1063 a_step = ImClamp(a_step, 1, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_TABLE_SIZE / 4);
1064
1065 const int sample_range = ImAbs(a_max_sample - a_min_sample);
1066 const int a_next_step = a_step;
1067
1068 int samples = sample_range + 1;
1069 bool extra_max_sample = false;
1070 if (a_step > 1)
1071 {
1072 samples = sample_range / a_step + 1;
1073 const int overstep = sample_range % a_step;
1074
1075 if (overstep > 0)
1076 {
1077 extra_max_sample = true;
1078 samples++;
1079
1080 // When we have overstep to avoid awkwardly looking one long line and one tiny one at the end,
1081 // distribute first step range evenly between them by reducing first step size.
1082 if (sample_range > 0)
1083 a_step -= (a_step - overstep) / 2;
1084 }
1085 }
1086
1087 _Path.resize(_Path.Size + samples);
1088 ImVec2* out_ptr = _Path.Data + (_Path.Size - samples);
1089
1090 int sample_index = a_min_sample;
1091 if (sample_index < 0 || sample_index >= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX)
1092 {
1093 sample_index = sample_index % IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1094 if (sample_index < 0)
1095 sample_index += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1096 }
1097
1098 if (a_max_sample >= a_min_sample)
1099 {
1100 for (int a = a_min_sample; a <= a_max_sample; a += a_step, sample_index += a_step, a_step = a_next_step)
1101 {
1102 // a_step is clamped to IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, so we have guaranteed that it will not wrap over range twice or more
1103 if (sample_index >= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX)
1104 sample_index -= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1105
1106 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[sample_index];
1107 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1108 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1109 out_ptr++;
1110 }
1111 }
1112 else
1113 {
1114 for (int a = a_min_sample; a >= a_max_sample; a -= a_step, sample_index -= a_step, a_step = a_next_step)
1115 {
1116 // a_step is clamped to IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, so we have guaranteed that it will not wrap over range twice or more
1117 if (sample_index < 0)
1118 sample_index += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1119
1120 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[sample_index];
1121 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1122 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1123 out_ptr++;
1124 }
1125 }
1126
1127 if (extra_max_sample)
1128 {
1129 int normalized_max_sample = a_max_sample % IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1130 if (normalized_max_sample < 0)
1131 normalized_max_sample += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1132
1133 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[normalized_max_sample];
1134 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1135 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1136 out_ptr++;
1137 }
1138
1139 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(_Path.Data + _Path.Size == out_ptr);
1140}
1141
1142void ImDrawList::_PathArcToN(const ImVec2& center, float radius, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1143{
1144 if (radius < 0.5f)
1145 {
1146 _Path.push_back(center);
1147 return;
1148 }
1149
1150 // Note that we are adding a point at both a_min and a_max.
1151 // If you are trying to draw a full closed circle you don't want the overlapping points!
1152 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (num_segments + 1));
1153 for (int i = 0; i <= num_segments; i++)
1154 {
1155 const float a = a_min + ((float)i / (float)num_segments) * (a_max - a_min);
1156 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a) * radius));
1157 }
1158}
1159
1160// 0: East, 3: South, 6: West, 9: North, 12: East
1161void ImDrawList::PathArcToFast(const ImVec2& center, float radius, int a_min_of_12, int a_max_of_12)
1162{
1163 if (radius < 0.5f)
1164 {
1165 _Path.push_back(center);
1166 return;
1167 }
1168 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, a_min_of_12 * IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / 12, a_max_of_12 * IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / 12, 0);
1169}
1170
1171void ImDrawList::PathArcTo(const ImVec2& center, float radius, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1172{
1173 if (radius < 0.5f)
1174 {
1175 _Path.push_back(center);
1176 return;
1177 }
1178
1179 if (num_segments > 0)
1180 {
1181 _PathArcToN(center, radius, a_min, a_max, num_segments);
1182 return;
1183 }
1184
1185 // Automatic segment count
1186 if (radius <= _Data->ArcFastRadiusCutoff)
1187 {
1188 const bool a_is_reverse = a_max < a_min;
1189
1190 // We are going to use precomputed values for mid samples.
1191 // Determine first and last sample in lookup table that belong to the arc.
1192 const float a_min_sample_f = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX * a_min / (IM_PI * 2.0f);
1193 const float a_max_sample_f = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX * a_max / (IM_PI * 2.0f);
1194
1195 const int a_min_sample = a_is_reverse ? (int)ImFloor(a_min_sample_f) : (int)ImCeil(a_min_sample_f);
1196 const int a_max_sample = a_is_reverse ? (int)ImCeil(a_max_sample_f) : (int)ImFloor(a_max_sample_f);
1197 const int a_mid_samples = a_is_reverse ? ImMax(a_min_sample - a_max_sample, 0) : ImMax(a_max_sample - a_min_sample, 0);
1198
1199 const float a_min_segment_angle = a_min_sample * IM_PI * 2.0f / IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1200 const float a_max_segment_angle = a_max_sample * IM_PI * 2.0f / IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1201 const bool a_emit_start = ImAbs(a_min_segment_angle - a_min) >= 1e-5f;
1202 const bool a_emit_end = ImAbs(a_max - a_max_segment_angle) >= 1e-5f;
1203
1204 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (a_mid_samples + 1 + (a_emit_start ? 1 : 0) + (a_emit_end ? 1 : 0)));
1205 if (a_emit_start)
1206 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a_min) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a_min) * radius));
1207 if (a_mid_samples > 0)
1208 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, a_min_sample, a_max_sample, 0);
1209 if (a_emit_end)
1210 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a_max) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a_max) * radius));
1211 }
1212 else
1213 {
1214 const float arc_length = ImAbs(a_max - a_min);
1215 const int circle_segment_count = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(radius);
1216 const int arc_segment_count = ImMax((int)ImCeil(circle_segment_count * arc_length / (IM_PI * 2.0f)), (int)(2.0f * IM_PI / arc_length));
1217 _PathArcToN(center, radius, a_min, a_max, arc_segment_count);
1218 }
1219}
1220
1221void ImDrawList::PathEllipticalArcTo(const ImVec2& center, const ImVec2& radius, float rot, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1222{
1223 if (num_segments <= 0)
1224 num_segments = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(ImMax(radius.x, radius.y)); // A bit pessimistic, maybe there's a better computation to do here.
1225
1226 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (num_segments + 1));
1227
1228 const float cos_rot = ImCos(rot);
1229 const float sin_rot = ImSin(rot);
1230 for (int i = 0; i <= num_segments; i++)
1231 {
1232 const float a = a_min + ((float)i / (float)num_segments) * (a_max - a_min);
1233 ImVec2 point(ImCos(a) * radius.x, ImSin(a) * radius.y);
1234 const ImVec2 rel((point.x * cos_rot) - (point.y * sin_rot), (point.x * sin_rot) + (point.y * cos_rot));
1235 point.x = rel.x + center.x;
1236 point.y = rel.y + center.y;
1237 _Path.push_back(point);
1238 }
1239}
1240
1241ImVec2 ImBezierCubicCalc(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, float t)
1242{
1243 float u = 1.0f - t;
1244 float w1 = u * u * u;
1245 float w2 = 3 * u * u * t;
1246 float w3 = 3 * u * t * t;
1247 float w4 = t * t * t;
1248 return ImVec2(w1 * p1.x + w2 * p2.x + w3 * p3.x + w4 * p4.x, w1 * p1.y + w2 * p2.y + w3 * p3.y + w4 * p4.y);
1249}
1250
1251ImVec2 ImBezierQuadraticCalc(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, float t)
1252{
1253 float u = 1.0f - t;
1254 float w1 = u * u;
1255 float w2 = 2 * u * t;
1256 float w3 = t * t;
1257 return ImVec2(w1 * p1.x + w2 * p2.x + w3 * p3.x, w1 * p1.y + w2 * p2.y + w3 * p3.y);
1258}
1259
1260// Closely mimics ImBezierCubicClosestPointCasteljau() in imgui.cpp
1261static void PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(ImVector<ImVec2>* path, float x1, float y1, float x2, float y2, float x3, float y3, float x4, float y4, float tess_tol, int level)
1262{
1263 float dx = x4 - x1;
1264 float dy = y4 - y1;
1265 float d2 = (x2 - x4) * dy - (y2 - y4) * dx;
1266 float d3 = (x3 - x4) * dy - (y3 - y4) * dx;
1267 d2 = (d2 >= 0) ? d2 : -d2;
1268 d3 = (d3 >= 0) ? d3 : -d3;
1269 if ((d2 + d3) * (d2 + d3) < tess_tol * (dx * dx + dy * dy))
1270 {
1271 path->push_back(ImVec2(x4, y4));
1272 }
1273 else if (level < 10)
1274 {
1275 float x12 = (x1 + x2) * 0.5f, y12 = (y1 + y2) * 0.5f;
1276 float x23 = (x2 + x3) * 0.5f, y23 = (y2 + y3) * 0.5f;
1277 float x34 = (x3 + x4) * 0.5f, y34 = (y3 + y4) * 0.5f;
1278 float x123 = (x12 + x23) * 0.5f, y123 = (y12 + y23) * 0.5f;
1279 float x234 = (x23 + x34) * 0.5f, y234 = (y23 + y34) * 0.5f;
1280 float x1234 = (x123 + x234) * 0.5f, y1234 = (y123 + y234) * 0.5f;
1281 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(path, x1, y1, x12, y12, x123, y123, x1234, y1234, tess_tol, level + 1);
1282 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(path, x1234, y1234, x234, y234, x34, y34, x4, y4, tess_tol, level + 1);
1283 }
1284}
1285
1286static void PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(ImVector<ImVec2>* path, float x1, float y1, float x2, float y2, float x3, float y3, float tess_tol, int level)
1287{
1288 float dx = x3 - x1, dy = y3 - y1;
1289 float det = (x2 - x3) * dy - (y2 - y3) * dx;
1290 if (det * det * 4.0f < tess_tol * (dx * dx + dy * dy))
1291 {
1292 path->push_back(ImVec2(x3, y3));
1293 }
1294 else if (level < 10)
1295 {
1296 float x12 = (x1 + x2) * 0.5f, y12 = (y1 + y2) * 0.5f;
1297 float x23 = (x2 + x3) * 0.5f, y23 = (y2 + y3) * 0.5f;
1298 float x123 = (x12 + x23) * 0.5f, y123 = (y12 + y23) * 0.5f;
1299 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(path, x1, y1, x12, y12, x123, y123, tess_tol, level + 1);
1300 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(path, x123, y123, x23, y23, x3, y3, tess_tol, level + 1);
1301 }
1302}
1303
1304void ImDrawList::PathBezierCubicCurveTo(const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, int num_segments)
1305{
1306 ImVec2 p1 = _Path.back();
1307 if (num_segments == 0)
1308 {
1309 IM_ASSERT(_Data->CurveTessellationTol > 0.0f);
1310 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(&_Path, p1.x, p1.y, p2.x, p2.y, p3.x, p3.y, p4.x, p4.y, _Data->CurveTessellationTol, 0); // Auto-tessellated
1311 }
1312 else
1313 {
1314 float t_step = 1.0f / (float)num_segments;
1315 for (int i_step = 1; i_step <= num_segments; i_step++)
1316 _Path.push_back(ImBezierCubicCalc(p1, p2, p3, p4, t_step * i_step));
1317 }
1318}
1319
1320void ImDrawList::PathBezierQuadraticCurveTo(const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, int num_segments)
1321{
1322 ImVec2 p1 = _Path.back();
1323 if (num_segments == 0)
1324 {
1325 IM_ASSERT(_Data->CurveTessellationTol > 0.0f);
1326 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(&_Path, p1.x, p1.y, p2.x, p2.y, p3.x, p3.y, _Data->CurveTessellationTol, 0);// Auto-tessellated
1327 }
1328 else
1329 {
1330 float t_step = 1.0f / (float)num_segments;
1331 for (int i_step = 1; i_step <= num_segments; i_step++)
1332 _Path.push_back(ImBezierQuadraticCalc(p1, p2, p3, t_step * i_step));
1333 }
1334}
1335
1336static inline ImDrawFlags FixRectCornerFlags(ImDrawFlags flags)
1337{
1338 /*
1339 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft == (1 << 4));
1340#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_OBSOLETE_FUNCTIONS
1341 // Obsoleted in 1.82 (from February 2021). This code was stripped/simplified and mostly commented in 1.90 (from September 2023)
1342 // - Legacy Support for hard coded ~0 (used to be a suggested equivalent to ImDrawCornerFlags_All)
1343 if (flags == ~0) { return ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll; }
1344 // - Legacy Support for hard coded 0x01 to 0x0F (matching 15 out of 16 old flags combinations). Read details in older version of this code.
1345 if (flags >= 0x01 && flags <= 0x0F) { return (flags << 4); }
1346 // We cannot support hard coded 0x00 with 'float rounding > 0.0f' --> replace with ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone or use 'float rounding = 0.0f'
1347#endif
1348 */
1349 // If this assert triggers, please update your code replacing hardcoded values with new ImDrawFlags_RoundCorners* values.
1350 // Note that ImDrawFlags_Closed (== 0x01) is an invalid flag for AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect() etc. anyway.
1351 // See details in 1.82 Changelog as well as 2021/03/12 and 2023/09/08 entries in "API BREAKING CHANGES" section.
1352 IM_ASSERT((flags & 0x0F) == 0 && "Misuse of legacy hardcoded ImDrawCornerFlags values!");
1353
1354 if ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == 0)
1355 flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll;
1356
1357 return flags;
1358}
1359
1360void ImDrawList::PathRect(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& b, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1361{
1362 if (rounding >= 0.5f)
1363 {
1364 flags = FixRectCornerFlags(flags);
1365 rounding = ImMin(rounding, ImFabs(b.x - a.x) * (((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTop) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTop) || ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottom) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottom) ? 0.5f : 1.0f) - 1.0f);
1366 rounding = ImMin(rounding, ImFabs(b.y - a.y) * (((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersLeft) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersLeft) || ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersRight) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersRight) ? 0.5f : 1.0f) - 1.0f);
1367 }
1368 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1369 {
1370 PathLineTo(a);
1371 PathLineTo(ImVec2(b.x, a.y));
1372 PathLineTo(b);
1373 PathLineTo(ImVec2(a.x, b.y));
1374 }
1375 else
1376 {
1377 const float rounding_tl = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1378 const float rounding_tr = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1379 const float rounding_br = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1380 const float rounding_bl = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1381 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(a.x + rounding_tl, a.y + rounding_tl), rounding_tl, 6, 9);
1382 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(b.x - rounding_tr, a.y + rounding_tr), rounding_tr, 9, 12);
1383 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(b.x - rounding_br, b.y - rounding_br), rounding_br, 0, 3);
1384 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(a.x + rounding_bl, b.y - rounding_bl), rounding_bl, 3, 6);
1385 }
1386}
1387
1388void ImDrawList::AddLine(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, ImU32 col, float thickness)
1389{
1390 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1391 return;
1392 PathLineTo(p1 + ImVec2(0.5f, 0.5f));
1393 PathLineTo(p2 + ImVec2(0.5f, 0.5f));
1394 PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
1395}
1396
1397// p_min = upper-left, p_max = lower-right
1398// Note we don't render 1 pixels sized rectangles properly.
1399void ImDrawList::AddRect(const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags, float thickness)
1400{
1401 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1402 return;
1403 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLines)
1404 PathRect(p_min + ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), p_max - ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), rounding, flags);
1405 else
1406 PathRect(p_min + ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), p_max - ImVec2(0.49f, 0.49f), rounding, flags); // Better looking lower-right corner and rounded non-AA shapes.
1407 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1408}
1409
1410void ImDrawList::AddRectFilled(const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1411{
1412 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1413 return;
1414 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1415 {
1416 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1417 PrimRect(p_min, p_max, col);
1418 }
1419 else
1420 {
1421 PathRect(p_min, p_max, rounding, flags);
1422 PathFillConvex(col);
1423 }
1424}
1425
1426// p_min = upper-left, p_max = lower-right
1427void ImDrawList::AddRectFilledMultiColor(const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, ImU32 col_upr_left, ImU32 col_upr_right, ImU32 col_bot_right, ImU32 col_bot_left)
1428{
1429 if (((col_upr_left | col_upr_right | col_bot_right | col_bot_left) & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1430 return;
1431
1432 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
1433 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1434 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 1)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2));
1435 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 3));
1436 PrimWriteVtx(p_min, uv, col_upr_left);
1437 PrimWriteVtx(ImVec2(p_max.x, p_min.y), uv, col_upr_right);
1438 PrimWriteVtx(p_max, uv, col_bot_right);
1439 PrimWriteVtx(ImVec2(p_min.x, p_max.y), uv, col_bot_left);
1440}

1487
1488void ImDrawList::AddCircle(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments, float thickness)
1489{
1490 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || radius < 0.5f)
1491 return;
1492
1493 if (num_segments <= 0)
1494 {
1495 // Use arc with automatic segment count
1496 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius - 0.5f, 0, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, 0);
1497 _Path.Size--;
1498 }
1499 else
1500 {
1501 // Explicit segment count (still clamp to avoid drawing insanely tessellated shapes)
1502 num_segments = ImClamp(num_segments, 3, IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_MAX);
1503
1504 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1505 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1506 PathArcTo(center, radius - 0.5f, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1507 }
1508
1509 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1510}
1511
1512void ImDrawList::AddCircleFilled(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments)
1513{
1514 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || radius < 0.5f)
1515 return;
1516
1517 if (num_segments <= 0)
1518 {
1519 // Use arc with automatic segment count
1520 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, 0, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, 0);
1521 _Path.Size--;
1522 }
1523 else
1524 {
1525 // Explicit segment count (still clamp to avoid drawing insanely tessellated shapes)
1526 num_segments = ImClamp(num_segments, 3, IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_MAX);
1527
1528 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1529 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1530 PathArcTo(center, radius, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1531 }
1532
1533 PathFillConvex(col);
1534}

1536// Guaranteed to honor 'num_segments'
1537void ImDrawList::AddNgon(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments, float thickness)
1538{
1539 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || num_segments <= 2)
1540 return;
1541

1543 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1544 PathArcTo(center, radius - 0.5f, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1545 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1546}

1556 PathArcTo(center, radius, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1557 PathFillConvex(col);
1558}

1560// Ellipse
1561void ImDrawList::AddEllipse(const ImVec2& center, const ImVec2& radius, ImU32 col, float rot, int num_segments, float thickness)
1562{
1563 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1564 return;
1565
1566 if (num_segments <= 0)
1567 num_segments = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(ImMax(radius.x, radius.y)); // A bit pessimistic, maybe there's a better computation to do here.
1568
1569 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1570 const float a_max = IM_PI * 2.0f * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1571 PathEllipticalArcTo(center, radius, rot, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1572 PathStroke(col, true, thickness);
1573}

1578 return;
1579
1580 if (num_segments <= 0)
1581 num_segments = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(ImMax(radius.x, radius.y)); // A bit pessimistic, maybe there's a better computation to do here.
1582
1583 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1584 const float a_max = IM_PI * 2.0f * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1585 PathEllipticalArcTo(center, radius, rot, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1586 PathFillConvex(col);
