1610
1611void ImDrawList::AddText(const ImFont* font, float font_size, const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end, float wrap_width, const ImVec4* cpu_fine_clip_rect)
1612{
1613 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1614 return;
1615
1616 // Accept null ranges
1617 if (text_begin == text_end || text_begin[0] == 0)
1618 return;
1619 if (text_end == NULL)
1620 text_end = text_begin + strlen(text_begin);
1621
1622 // Pull default font/size from the shared ImDrawListSharedData instance
1623 if (font == NULL)
1624 font = _Data->Font;
1625 if (font_size == 0.0f)
1626 font_size = _Data->FontSize;
1627
1628 IM_ASSERT(font->ContainerAtlas->TexID == _CmdHeader.TextureId); // Use high-level ImGui::PushFont() or low-level ImDrawList::PushTextureId() to change font.
1629
1630 ImVec4 clip_rect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
1631 if (cpu_fine_clip_rect)
1632 {
1633 clip_rect.x = ImMax(clip_rect.x, cpu_fine_clip_rect->x);
1634 clip_rect.y = ImMax(clip_rect.y, cpu_fine_clip_rect->y);
1635 clip_rect.z = ImMin(clip_rect.z, cpu_fine_clip_rect->z);
1636 clip_rect.w = ImMin(clip_rect.w, cpu_fine_clip_rect->w);
1637 }
1638 font->RenderText(this, font_size, pos, col, clip_rect, text_begin, text_end, wrap_width, cpu_fine_clip_rect != NULL);
1639}
1640
1641void ImDrawList::AddText(const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end)
1642{
1643 AddText(NULL, 0.0f, pos, col, text_begin, text_end);
1644}
1645
1646void ImDrawList::AddImage(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, const ImVec2& uv_min, const ImVec2& uv_max, ImU32 col)
1647{
1648 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1649 return;
1650
1651 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1652 if (push_texture_id)
1653 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1654
1655 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1656 PrimRectUV(p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, col);
1657
1658 if (push_texture_id)
1659 PopTextureID();
1660}
1661
1662void ImDrawList::AddImageQuad(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, const ImVec2& uv1, const ImVec2& uv2, const ImVec2& uv3, const ImVec2& uv4, ImU32 col)
1663{
1664 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1665 return;
1666
1667 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1668 if (push_texture_id)
1669 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1670
1671 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1672 PrimQuadUV(p1, p2, p3, p4, uv1, uv2, uv3, uv4, col);
1673
1674 if (push_texture_id)
1675 PopTextureID();
1676}
1677
1678void ImDrawList::AddImageRounded(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, const ImVec2& uv_min, const ImVec2& uv_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1679{
1680 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1681 return;
1682
1683 flags = FixRectCornerFlags(flags);
1684 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1685 {
1686 AddImage(user_texture_id, p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, col);
1687 return;
1688 }
1689
1690 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1691 if (push_texture_id)
1692 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1693
1694 int vert_start_idx = VtxBuffer.Size;
1695 PathRect(p_min, p_max, rounding, flags);
1696 PathFillConvex(col);
1697 int vert_end_idx = VtxBuffer.Size;
1698 ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearUV(this, vert_start_idx, vert_end_idx, p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, true);
1699
1700 if (push_texture_id)
1701 PopTextureID();
1702}
1703
1704//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1705// [SECTION] ImTriangulator, ImDrawList concave polygon fill
1706//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1707// Triangulate concave polygons. Based on "Triangulation by Ear Clipping" paper, O(N^2) complexity.
1708// Reference: https://www.geometrictools.com/Documentation/TriangulationByEarClipping.pdf
1709// Provided as a convenience for user but not used by main library.
1710//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1711// - ImTriangulator [Internal]
1712// - AddConcavePolyFilled()
1713//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1714
1715enum ImTriangulatorNodeType
1716{
1717 ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex,
1718 ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear,
1719 ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex
1720};
1721
1722struct ImTriangulatorNode
1723{
1724 ImTriangulatorNodeType Type;
1725 int Index;
1726 ImVec2 Pos;
1727 ImTriangulatorNode* Next;
1728 ImTriangulatorNode* Prev;
1729
1730 void Unlink() { Next->Prev = Prev; Prev->Next = Next; }
1731};
1732
1733struct ImTriangulatorNodeSpan
1734{
1735 ImTriangulatorNode** Data = NULL;
1736 int Size = 0;
1737
1738 void push_back(ImTriangulatorNode* node) { Data[Size++] = node; }
1739 void find_erase_unsorted(int idx) { for (int i = Size - 1; i >= 0; i--) if (Data[i]->Index == idx) { Data[i] = Data[Size - 1]; Size--; return; } }
1740};
1741
1742struct ImTriangulator
1743{
1744 static int EstimateTriangleCount(int points_count) { return (points_count < 3) ? 0 : points_count - 2; }
1745 static int EstimateScratchBufferSize(int points_count) { return sizeof(ImTriangulatorNode) * points_count + sizeof(ImTriangulatorNode*) * points_count * 2; }
1746
1747 void Init(const ImVec2* points, int points_count, void* scratch_buffer);
1748 void GetNextTriangle(unsigned int out_triangle[3]); // Return relative indexes for next triangle
1749
1750 // Internal functions
1751 void BuildNodes(const ImVec2* points, int points_count);
1752 void BuildReflexes();
1753 void BuildEars();
1754 void FlipNodeList();
1755 bool IsEar(int i0, int i1, int i2, const ImVec2& v0, const ImVec2& v1, const ImVec2& v2) const;
1756 void ReclassifyNode(ImTriangulatorNode* node);
1757
1758 // Internal members
1759 int _TrianglesLeft = 0;
1760 ImTriangulatorNode* _Nodes = NULL;
1761 ImTriangulatorNodeSpan _Ears;
1762 ImTriangulatorNodeSpan _Reflexes;
1763};
1764
1765// Distribute storage for nodes, ears and reflexes.
1766// FIXME-OPT: if everything is convex, we could report it to caller and let it switch to an convex renderer
1767// (this would require first building reflexes to bail to convex if empty, without even building nodes)
1768void ImTriangulator::Init(const ImVec2* points, int points_count, void* scratch_buffer)
1769{
1770 IM_ASSERT(scratch_buffer != NULL && points_count >= 3);
1771 _TrianglesLeft = EstimateTriangleCount(points_count);
1772 _Nodes = (ImTriangulatorNode*)scratch_buffer; // points_count x Node
1773 _Ears.Data = (ImTriangulatorNode**)(_Nodes + points_count); // points_count x Node*
1774 _Reflexes.Data = (ImTriangulatorNode**)(_Nodes + points_count) + points_count; // points_count x Node*
1775 BuildNodes(points, points_count);
1776 BuildReflexes();
1777 BuildEars();
1778}
1779
1780void ImTriangulator::BuildNodes(const ImVec2* points, int points_count)
1781{
1782 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
1783 {
1784 _Nodes[i].Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex;
1785 _Nodes[i].Index = i;
1786 _Nodes[i].Pos = points[i];
1787 _Nodes[i].Next = _Nodes + i + 1;
1788 _Nodes[i].Prev = _Nodes + i - 1;
1789 }
1790 _Nodes[0].Prev = _Nodes + points_count - 1;
1791 _Nodes[points_count - 1].Next = _Nodes;
1792}
1793
1794void ImTriangulator::BuildReflexes()
1795{
1796 ImTriangulatorNode* n1 = _Nodes;
1797 for (int i = _TrianglesLeft; i >= 0; i--, n1 = n1->Next)
1798 {
1799 if (ImTriangleIsClockwise(n1->Prev->Pos, n1->Pos, n1->Next->Pos))
1800 continue;
1801 n1->Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex;
1802 _Reflexes.push_back(n1);
1803 }
1804}
1805
1806void ImTriangulator::BuildEars()
1807{
1808 ImTriangulatorNode* n1 = _Nodes;
1809 for (int i = _TrianglesLeft; i >= 0; i--, n1 = n1->Next)
1810 {
1811 if (n1->Type != ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex)
1812 continue;
1813 if (!IsEar(n1->Prev->Index, n1->Index, n1->Next->Index, n1->Prev->Pos, n1->Pos, n1->Next->Pos))
1814 continue;
1815 n1->Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear;
1816 _Ears.push_back(n1);
1817 }
1818}
1819
1820void ImTriangulator::GetNextTriangle(unsigned int out_triangle[3])
1821{
1822 if (_Ears.Size == 0)
1823 {
1824 FlipNodeList();
1825
1826 ImTriangulatorNode* node = _Nodes;
1827 for (int i = _TrianglesLeft; i >= 0; i--, node = node->Next)
1828 node->Type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex;
1829 _Reflexes.Size = 0;
1830 BuildReflexes();
1831 BuildEars();
1832
1833 // If we still don't have ears, it means geometry is degenerated.
1834 if (_Ears.Size == 0)
1835 {
1836 // Return first triangle available, mimicking the behavior of convex fill.
1837 IM_ASSERT(_TrianglesLeft > 0); // Geometry is degenerated
1838 _Ears.Data[0] = _Nodes;
1839 _Ears.Size = 1;
1840 }
1841 }
1842
1843 ImTriangulatorNode* ear = _Ears.Data[--_Ears.Size];
1844 out_triangle[0] = ear->Prev->Index;
1845 out_triangle[1] = ear->Index;
1846 out_triangle[2] = ear->Next->Index;
1847
1848 ear->Unlink();
1849 if (ear == _Nodes)
1850 _Nodes = ear->Next;
1851
1852 ReclassifyNode(ear->Prev);
1853 ReclassifyNode(ear->Next);
1854 _TrianglesLeft--;
1855}
1856
1857void ImTriangulator::FlipNodeList()
1858{
1859 ImTriangulatorNode* prev = _Nodes;
1860 ImTriangulatorNode* temp = _Nodes;
1861 ImTriangulatorNode* current = _Nodes->Next;
1862 prev->Next = prev;
1863 prev->Prev = prev;
1864 while (current != _Nodes)
1865 {
1866 temp = current->Next;
1867
1868 current->Next = prev;
1869 prev->Prev = current;
1870 _Nodes->Next = current;
1871 current->Prev = _Nodes;
1872
1873 prev = current;
1874 current = temp;
1875 }
1876 _Nodes = prev;
1877}
1878
1879// A triangle is an ear is no other vertex is inside it. We can test reflexes vertices only (see reference algorithm)
1880bool ImTriangulator::IsEar(int i0, int i1, int i2, const ImVec2& v0, const ImVec2& v1, const ImVec2& v2) const
1881{
1882 ImTriangulatorNode** p_end = _Reflexes.Data + _Reflexes.Size;
1883 for (ImTriangulatorNode** p = _Reflexes.Data; p < p_end; p++)
1884 {
1885 ImTriangulatorNode* reflex = *p;
1886 if (reflex->Index != i0 && reflex->Index != i1 && reflex->Index != i2)
1887 if (ImTriangleContainsPoint(v0, v1, v2, reflex->Pos))
1888 return false;
1889 }
1890 return true;
1891}
1892
1893void ImTriangulator::ReclassifyNode(ImTriangulatorNode* n1)
1894{
1895 // Classify node
1896 ImTriangulatorNodeType type;
1897 const ImTriangulatorNode* n0 = n1->Prev;
1898 const ImTriangulatorNode* n2 = n1->Next;
1899 if (!ImTriangleIsClockwise(n0->Pos, n1->Pos, n2->Pos))
1900 type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex;
1901 else if (IsEar(n0->Index, n1->Index, n2->Index, n0->Pos, n1->Pos, n2->Pos))
1902 type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear;
1903 else
1904 type = ImTriangulatorNodeType_Convex;
1905
1906 // Update lists when a type changes
1907 if (type == n1->Type)
1908 return;
1909 if (n1->Type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex)
1910 _Reflexes.find_erase_unsorted(n1->Index);
1911 else if (n1->Type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear)
1912 _Ears.find_erase_unsorted(n1->Index);
1913 if (type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Reflex)
1914 _Reflexes.push_back(n1);
1915 else if (type == ImTriangulatorNodeType_Ear)
1916 _Ears.push_back(n1);
1917 n1->Type = type;
1918}
1919
1920// Use ear-clipping algorithm to triangulate a simple polygon (no self-interaction, no holes).
1921// (Reminder: we don't perform any coarse clipping/culling in ImDrawList layer!
1922// It is up to caller to ensure not making costly calls that will be outside of visible area.
1923// As concave fill is noticeably more expensive than other primitives, be mindful of this...
1924// Caller can build AABB of points, and avoid filling if 'draw_list->_CmdHeader.ClipRect.Overlays(points_bb) == false')
1925void ImDrawList::AddConcavePolyFilled(const ImVec2* points, const int points_count, ImU32 col)
1926{
1927 if (points_count < 3 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1928 return;
1929
1930 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
1931 ImTriangulator triangulator;
1932 unsigned int triangle[3];
1933 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedFill)
1934 {
1935 // Anti-aliased Fill
1936 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
1937 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
1938 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2) * 3 + points_count * 6;
1939 const int vtx_count = (points_count * 2);
1940 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1941
1942 // Add indexes for fill
1943 unsigned int vtx_inner_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx;
1944 unsigned int vtx_outer_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx + 1;
1945
1946 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard((ImTriangulator::EstimateScratchBufferSize(points_count) + sizeof(ImVec2)) / sizeof(ImVec2));
1947 triangulator.Init(points, points_count, _Data->TempBuffer.Data);
1948 while (triangulator._TrianglesLeft > 0)
1949 {
1950 triangulator.GetNextTriangle(triangle);
1951 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (triangle[0] << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (triangle[1] << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (triangle[2] << 1));
1952 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
1953 }
1954
1955 // Compute normals
1956 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count);
1957 ImVec2* temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
1958 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
1959 {
1960 const ImVec2& p0 = points[i0];
1961 const ImVec2& p1 = points[i1];
1962 float dx = p1.x - p0.x;
1963 float dy = p1.y - p0.y;
1964 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
1965 temp_normals[i0].x = dy;
1966 temp_normals[i0].y = -dx;
1967 }
1968
1969 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
1970 {
1971 // Average normals
1972 const ImVec2& n0 = temp_normals[i0];
1973 const ImVec2& n1 = temp_normals[i1];
1974 float dm_x = (n0.x + n1.x) * 0.5f;
1975 float dm_y = (n0.y + n1.y) * 0.5f;
1976 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
1977 dm_x *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1978 dm_y *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1979
1980 // Add vertices
1981 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = (points[i1].x - dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = (points[i1].y - dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Inner
1982 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = (points[i1].x + dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = (points[i1].y + dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Outer
1983 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
1984
1985 // Add indexes for fringes
1986 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1));
1987 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1));
1988 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
1989 }
1990 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1991 }
1992 else
1993 {
1994 // Non Anti-aliased Fill
1995 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2) * 3;
1996 const int vtx_count = points_count;
1997 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1998 for (int i = 0; i < vtx_count; i++)
1999 {
2000 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
2001 _VtxWritePtr++;
2002 }
2003 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard((ImTriangulator::EstimateScratchBufferSize(points_count) + sizeof(ImVec2)) / sizeof(ImVec2));
2004 triangulator.Init(points, points_count, _Data->TempBuffer.Data);
2005 while (triangulator._TrianglesLeft > 0)
2006 {
2007 triangulator.GetNextTriangle(triangle);
2008 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + triangle[0]); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + triangle[1]); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + triangle[2]);
2009 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
2010 }
2011 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
2012 }
2013}
2014
2015//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2016// [SECTION] ImDrawListSplitter
2017//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2018// FIXME: This may be a little confusing, trying to be a little too low-level/optimal instead of just doing vector swap..
2019//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2020
2021void ImDrawListSplitter::ClearFreeMemory()
2022{
2023 for (int i = 0; i < _Channels.Size; i++)
2024 {
2025 if (i == _Current)
2026 memset(&_Channels[i], 0, sizeof(_Channels[i])); // Current channel is a copy of CmdBuffer/IdxBuffer, don't destruct again
2027 _Channels[i]._CmdBuffer.clear();
2028 _Channels[i]._IdxBuffer.clear();
2029 }
2030 _Current = 0;
2031 _Count = 1;
2032 _Channels.clear();
2033}
2034
2035void ImDrawListSplitter::Split(ImDrawList* draw_list, int channels_count)
2036{
2037 IM_UNUSED(draw_list);
2038 IM_ASSERT(_Current == 0 && _Count <= 1 && "Nested channel splitting is not supported. Please use separate instances of ImDrawListSplitter.");
2039 int old_channels_count = _Channels.Size;
2040 if (old_channels_count < channels_count)
2041 {
2042 _Channels.reserve(channels_count); // Avoid over reserving since this is likely to stay stable
2043 _Channels.resize(channels_count);
2044 }
2045 _Count = channels_count;
2046
2047 // Channels[] (24/32 bytes each) hold storage that we'll swap with draw_list->_CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer
2048 // The content of Channels[0] at this point doesn't matter. We clear it to make state tidy in a debugger but we don't strictly need to.
2049 // When we switch to the next channel, we'll copy draw_list->_CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer into Channels[0] and then Channels[1] into draw_list->CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer
2050 memset(&_Channels[0], 0, sizeof(ImDrawChannel));
2051 for (int i = 1; i < channels_count; i++)
2052 {
2053 if (i >= old_channels_count)
2054 {
2055 IM_PLACEMENT_NEW(&_Channels[i]) ImDrawChannel();
2056 }
2057 else
2058 {
2059 _Channels[i]._CmdBuffer.resize(0);
2060 _Channels[i]._IdxBuffer.resize(0);
2061 }
2062 }
2063}
2064
2065void ImDrawListSplitter::Merge(ImDrawList* draw_list)
2066{
2067 // Note that we never use or rely on _Channels.Size because it is merely a buffer that we never shrink back to 0 to keep all sub-buffers ready for use.
2068 if (_Count <= 1)
2069 return;
2070
2071 SetCurrentChannel(draw_list, 0);
2072 draw_list->_PopUnusedDrawCmd();
2073
2074 // Calculate our final buffer sizes. Also fix the incorrect IdxOffset values in each command.
2075 int new_cmd_buffer_count = 0;
2076 int new_idx_buffer_count = 0;
2077 ImDrawCmd* last_cmd = (_Count > 0 && draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size > 0) ? &draw_list->CmdBuffer.back() : NULL;
2078 int idx_offset = last_cmd ? last_cmd->IdxOffset + last_cmd->ElemCount : 0;
2079 for (int i = 1; i < _Count; i++)
2080 {
2081 ImDrawChannel& ch = _Channels[i];
2082 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && ch._CmdBuffer.back().ElemCount == 0 && ch._CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback == NULL) // Equivalent of PopUnusedDrawCmd()
2083 ch._CmdBuffer.pop_back();
2084
2085 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && last_cmd != NULL)
2086 {
2087 // Do not include ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset() in the compare as we rebuild IdxOffset values ourselves.
2088 // Manipulating IdxOffset (e.g. by reordering draw commands like done by RenderDimmedBackgroundBehindWindow()) is not supported within a splitter.
2089 ImDrawCmd* next_cmd = &ch._CmdBuffer[0];
2090 if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(last_cmd, next_cmd) == 0 && last_cmd->UserCallback == NULL && next_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
2091 {
2092 // Merge previous channel last draw command with current channel first draw command if matching.
2093 last_cmd->ElemCount += next_cmd->ElemCount;
2094 idx_offset += next_cmd->ElemCount;
2095 ch._CmdBuffer.erase(ch._CmdBuffer.Data); // FIXME-OPT: Improve for multiple merges.
2096 }
2097 }
2098 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0)
2099 last_cmd = &ch._CmdBuffer.back();
2100 new_cmd_buffer_count += ch._CmdBuffer.Size;
2101 new_idx_buffer_count += ch._IdxBuffer.Size;
2102 for (int cmd_n = 0; cmd_n < ch._CmdBuffer.Size; cmd_n++)
2103 {
2104 ch._CmdBuffer.Data[cmd_n].IdxOffset = idx_offset;
2105 idx_offset += ch._CmdBuffer.Data[cmd_n].ElemCount;
2106 }
2107 }
2108 draw_list->CmdBuffer.resize(draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size + new_cmd_buffer_count);
2109 draw_list->IdxBuffer.resize(draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size + new_idx_buffer_count);
2110
2111 // Write commands and indices in order (they are fairly small structures, we don't copy vertices only indices)
2112 ImDrawCmd* cmd_write = draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data + draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - new_cmd_buffer_count;
2113 ImDrawIdx* idx_write = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size - new_idx_buffer_count;
2114 for (int i = 1; i < _Count; i++)
2115 {
2116 ImDrawChannel& ch = _Channels[i];
2117 if (int sz = ch._CmdBuffer.Size) { memcpy(cmd_write, ch._CmdBuffer.Data, sz * sizeof(ImDrawCmd)); cmd_write += sz; }
2118 if (int sz = ch._IdxBuffer.Size) { memcpy(idx_write, ch._IdxBuffer.Data, sz * sizeof(ImDrawIdx)); idx_write += sz; }
2119 }
2120 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = idx_write;
2121
2122 // Ensure there's always a non-callback draw command trailing the command-buffer
2123 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0 || draw_list->CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback != NULL)
2124 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2125
2126 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
2127 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
2128 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0)
2129 ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader); // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
2130 else if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader) != 0)
2131 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2132
2133 _Count = 1;
2134}
2135
2136void ImDrawListSplitter::SetCurrentChannel(ImDrawList* draw_list, int idx)
2137{
2138 IM_ASSERT(idx >= 0 && idx < _Count);
2139 if (_Current == idx)
2140 return;
2141
2142 // Overwrite ImVector (12/16 bytes), four times. This is merely a silly optimization instead of doing .swap()
2143 memcpy(&_Channels.Data[_Current]._CmdBuffer, &draw_list->CmdBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->CmdBuffer));
2144 memcpy(&_Channels.Data[_Current]._IdxBuffer, &draw_list->IdxBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->IdxBuffer));
2145 _Current = idx;
2146 memcpy(&draw_list->CmdBuffer, &_Channels.Data[idx]._CmdBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->CmdBuffer));
2147 memcpy(&draw_list->IdxBuffer, &_Channels.Data[idx]._IdxBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->IdxBuffer));
2148 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size;
2149
2150 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
2151 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0) ? NULL : &draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
2152 if (curr_cmd == NULL)
2153 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2154 else if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0)
2155 ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader); // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
2156 else if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader) != 0)
2157 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
2158}
2159
2160//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2161// [SECTION] ImDrawData
2162//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2163
2164void ImDrawData::Clear()
2165{
2166 Valid = false;
2167 CmdListsCount = TotalIdxCount = TotalVtxCount = 0;
2168 CmdLists.resize(0); // The ImDrawList are NOT owned by ImDrawData but e.g. by ImGuiContext, so we don't clear them.
2169 DisplayPos = DisplaySize = FramebufferScale = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
2170 OwnerViewport = NULL;
2171}
2172
2173// Important: 'out_list' is generally going to be draw_data->CmdLists, but may be another temporary list
2174// as long at it is expected that the result will be later merged into draw_data->CmdLists[].
2175void ImGui::AddDrawListToDrawDataEx(ImDrawData* draw_data, ImVector<ImDrawList*>* out_list, ImDrawList* draw_list)
2176{
2177 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0)
2178 return;
2179 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 1 && draw_list->CmdBuffer[0].ElemCount == 0 && draw_list->CmdBuffer[0].UserCallback == NULL)
2180 return;
2181
2182 // Draw list sanity check. Detect mismatch between PrimReserve() calls and incrementing _VtxCurrentIdx, _VtxWritePtr etc.
2183 // May trigger for you if you are using PrimXXX functions incorrectly.
2184 IM_ASSERT(draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size == 0 || draw_list->_VtxWritePtr == draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size);
2185 IM_ASSERT(draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size == 0 || draw_list->_IdxWritePtr == draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
2186 if (!(draw_list->Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AllowVtxOffset))
2187 IM_ASSERT((int)draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx == draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size);
2188
2189 // Check that draw_list doesn't use more vertices than indexable (default ImDrawIdx = unsigned short = 2 bytes = 64K vertices per ImDrawList = per window)
2190 // If this assert triggers because you are drawing lots of stuff manually:
2191 // - First, make sure you are coarse clipping yourself and not trying to draw many things outside visible bounds.
2192 // Be mindful that the lower-level ImDrawList API doesn't filter vertices. Use the Metrics/Debugger window to inspect draw list contents.
2193 // - If you want large meshes with more than 64K vertices, you can either:
2194 // (A) Handle the ImDrawCmd::VtxOffset value in your renderer backend, and set 'io.BackendFlags |= ImGuiBackendFlags_RendererHasVtxOffset'.
2195 // Most example backends already support this from 1.71. Pre-1.71 backends won't.
2196 // Some graphics API such as GL ES 1/2 don't have a way to offset the starting vertex so it is not supported for them.
2197 // (B) Or handle 32-bit indices in your renderer backend, and uncomment '#define ImDrawIdx unsigned int' line in imconfig.h.
2198 // Most example backends already support this. For example, the OpenGL example code detect index size at compile-time:
2199 // glDrawElements(GL_TRIANGLES, (GLsizei)pcmd->ElemCount, sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2 ? GL_UNSIGNED_SHORT : GL_UNSIGNED_INT, idx_buffer_offset);
2200 // Your own engine or render API may use different parameters or function calls to specify index sizes.
2201 // 2 and 4 bytes indices are generally supported by most graphics API.
2202 // - If for some reason neither of those solutions works for you, a workaround is to call BeginChild()/EndChild() before reaching
2203 // the 64K limit to split your draw commands in multiple draw lists.
2204 if (sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2)
2205 IM_ASSERT(draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx < (1 << 16) && "Too many vertices in ImDrawList using 16-bit indices. Read comment above");
2206
2207 // Add to output list + records state in ImDrawData
2208 out_list->push_back(draw_list);
2209 draw_data->CmdListsCount++;
2210 draw_data->TotalVtxCount += draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size;
2211 draw_data->TotalIdxCount += draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size;
2212}
2213
2214void ImDrawData::AddDrawList(ImDrawList* draw_list)
2215{
2216 IM_ASSERT(CmdLists.Size == CmdListsCount);
2217 draw_list->_PopUnusedDrawCmd();
2218 ImGui::AddDrawListToDrawDataEx(this, &CmdLists, draw_list);
2219}
2220
2221// For backward compatibility: convert all buffers from indexed to de-indexed, in case you cannot render indexed. Note: this is slow and most likely a waste of resources. Always prefer indexed rendering!
2222void ImDrawData::DeIndexAllBuffers()
2223{
2224 ImVector<ImDrawVert> new_vtx_buffer;
2225 TotalVtxCount = TotalIdxCount = 0;
2226 for (int i = 0; i < CmdListsCount; i++)
2227 {
2228 ImDrawList* cmd_list = CmdLists[i];
2229 if (cmd_list->IdxBuffer.empty())
2230 continue;
2231 new_vtx_buffer.resize(cmd_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
2232 for (int j = 0; j < cmd_list->IdxBuffer.Size; j++)
2233 new_vtx_buffer[j] = cmd_list->VtxBuffer[cmd_list->IdxBuffer[j]];
2234 cmd_list->VtxBuffer.swap(new_vtx_buffer);
2235 cmd_list->IdxBuffer.resize(0);
2236 TotalVtxCount += cmd_list->VtxBuffer.Size;
2237 }
2238}
2239
2240// Helper to scale the ClipRect field of each ImDrawCmd.
2241// Use if your final output buffer is at a different scale than draw_data->DisplaySize,
2242// or if there is a difference between your window resolution and framebuffer resolution.
2243void ImDrawData::ScaleClipRects(const ImVec2& fb_scale)
2244{
2245 for (ImDrawList* draw_list : CmdLists)
2246 for (ImDrawCmd& cmd : draw_list->CmdBuffer)
2247 cmd.ClipRect = ImVec4(cmd.ClipRect.x * fb_scale.x, cmd.ClipRect.y * fb_scale.y, cmd.ClipRect.z * fb_scale.x, cmd.ClipRect.w * fb_scale.y);
2248}
2249
2250//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2251// [SECTION] Helpers ShadeVertsXXX functions
2252//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
2253
2254// Generic linear color gradient, write to RGB fields, leave A untouched.
2255void ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearColorGradientKeepAlpha(ImDrawList* draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, ImVec2 gradient_p0, ImVec2 gradient_p1, ImU32 col0, ImU32 col1)
2256{
2257 ImVec2 gradient_extent = gradient_p1 - gradient_p0;
2258 float gradient_inv_length2 = 1.0f / ImLengthSqr(gradient_extent);
2259 ImDrawVert* vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
2260 ImDrawVert* vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
2261 const int col0_r = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
2262 const int col0_g = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
2263 const int col0_b = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
2264 const int col_delta_r = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_r;
2265 const int col_delta_g = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_g;
2266 const int col_delta_b = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_b;
2267 for (ImDrawVert* vert = vert_start; vert < vert_end; vert++)
2268 {
2269 float d = ImDot(vert->pos - gradient_p0, gradient_extent);
2270 float t = ImClamp(d * gradient_inv_length2, 0.0f, 1.0f);
2271 int r = (int)(col0_r + col_delta_r * t);
2272 int g = (int)(col0_g + col_delta_g * t);
2273 int b = (int)(col0_b + col_delta_b * t);
2274 vert->col = (r << IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) | (g << IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) | (b << IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) | (vert->col & IM_COL32_A_MASK);
2275 }
2276}
2277
2278// Distribute UV over (a, b) rectangle
2279void ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearUV(ImDrawList* draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& b, const ImVec2& uv_a, const ImVec2& uv_b, bool clamp)
2280{
2281 const ImVec2 size = b - a;
2282 const ImVec2 uv_size = uv_b - uv_a;
2283 const ImVec2 scale = ImVec2(
2284 size.x != 0.0f ? (uv_size.x / size.x) : 0.0f,
2285 size.y != 0.0f ? (uv_size.y / size.y) : 0.0f);
2286
2287 ImDrawVert* vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
2288 ImDrawVert* vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
2289 if (clamp)
2290 {
2291 const ImVec2 min = ImMin(uv_a, uv_b);
2292 const ImVec2 max = ImMax(uv_a, uv_b);
2293 for (ImDrawVert* vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
2294 vertex->uv = ImClamp(uv_a + ImMul(ImVec2(vertex->pos.x, vertex->pos.y) - a, scale), min, max);
2295 }
2296 else
2297 {
2298 for (ImDrawVert* vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
2299 vertex->uv = uv_a + ImMul(ImVec2(vertex->pos.x, vertex->pos.y) - a, scale);
2300 }
2301}
2302
2303void ImGui::ShadeVertsTransformPos(ImDrawList* draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, const ImVec2& pivot_in, float cos_a, float sin_a, const ImVec2& pivot_out)
2304{
2305 ImDrawVert* vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
2306 ImDrawVert* vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
2307 for (ImDrawVert* vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
2308 vertex->pos = ImRotate(vertex->pos- pivot_in, cos_a, sin_a) + pivot_out;
2309}

2386}

2388ImFontAtlas::~ImFontAtlas()
2389{
2390 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2391 Clear();
2392}
2393
2394void ImFontAtlas::ClearInputData()
2395{
2396 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2397 for (ImFontConfig& font_cfg : ConfigData)
2398 if (font_cfg.FontData && font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas)
2399 {
2400 IM_FREE(font_cfg.FontData);
2401 font_cfg.FontData = NULL;
2402 }
2403
2404 // When clearing this we lose access to the font name and other information used to build the font.
2405 for (ImFont* font : Fonts)
2406 if (font->ConfigData >= ConfigData.Data && font->ConfigData < ConfigData.Data + ConfigData.Size)
2407 {
2408 font->ConfigData = NULL;
2409 font->ConfigDataCount = 0;
2410 }
2411 ConfigData.clear();
2412 CustomRects.clear();
2413 PackIdMouseCursors = PackIdLines = -1;
2414 // Important: we leave TexReady untouched
2415}
2416
2417void ImFontAtlas::ClearTexData()
2418{
2419 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2420 if (TexPixelsAlpha8)
2421 IM_FREE(TexPixelsAlpha8);
2422 if (TexPixelsRGBA32)
2423 IM_FREE(TexPixelsRGBA32);
2424 TexPixelsAlpha8 = NULL;
2425 TexPixelsRGBA32 = NULL;
2426 TexPixelsUseColors = false;
2427 // Important: we leave TexReady untouched
2428}
2429
2430void ImFontAtlas::ClearFonts()
2431{
2432 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2433 Fonts.clear_delete();
2434 TexReady = false;
2435}
2436
2437void ImFontAtlas::Clear()
2438{
2439 ClearInputData();
2440 ClearTexData();
2441 ClearFonts();
2442}
2443
2444void ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAsAlpha8(unsigned char** out_pixels, int* out_width, int* out_height, int* out_bytes_per_pixel)
2445{
2446 // Build atlas on demand
2447 if (TexPixelsAlpha8 == NULL)
2448 Build();
2449
2450 *out_pixels = TexPixelsAlpha8;
2451 if (out_width) *out_width = TexWidth;
2452 if (out_height) *out_height = TexHeight;
2453 if (out_bytes_per_pixel) *out_bytes_per_pixel = 1;
2454}
2455
2456void ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAsRGBA32(unsigned char** out_pixels, int* out_width, int* out_height, int* out_bytes_per_pixel)
2457{
2458 // Convert to RGBA32 format on demand
2459 // Although it is likely to be the most commonly used format, our font rendering is 1 channel / 8 bpp
2460 if (!TexPixelsRGBA32)
2461 {
2462 unsigned char* pixels = NULL;
2463 GetTexDataAsAlpha8(&pixels, NULL, NULL);
2464 if (pixels)
2465 {
2466 TexPixelsRGBA32 = (unsigned int*)IM_ALLOC((size_t)TexWidth * (size_t)TexHeight * 4);
2467 const unsigned char* src = pixels;
2468 unsigned int* dst = TexPixelsRGBA32;
2469 for (int n = TexWidth * TexHeight; n > 0; n--)
2470 *dst++ = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, (unsigned int)(*src++));
2471 }
2472 }
2473
2474 *out_pixels = (unsigned char*)TexPixelsRGBA32;
2475 if (out_width) *out_width = TexWidth;
2476 if (out_height) *out_height = TexHeight;
2477 if (out_bytes_per_pixel) *out_bytes_per_pixel = 4;
2478}
2479
2480ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFont(const ImFontConfig* font_cfg)
2481{
2482 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2483 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->FontData != NULL && font_cfg->FontDataSize > 0);
2484 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->SizePixels > 0.0f);
2485
2486 // Create new font
2487 if (!font_cfg->MergeMode)
2488 Fonts.push_back(IM_NEW(ImFont));
2489 else
2490 IM_ASSERT(!Fonts.empty() && "Cannot use MergeMode for the first font"); // When using MergeMode make sure that a font has already been added before. You can use ImGui::GetIO().Fonts->AddFontDefault() to add the default imgui font.
2491
2492 ConfigData.push_back(*font_cfg);
2493 ImFontConfig& new_font_cfg = ConfigData.back();
2494 if (new_font_cfg.DstFont == NULL)
2495 new_font_cfg.DstFont = Fonts.back();
2496 if (!new_font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas)
2497 {
2498 new_font_cfg.FontData = IM_ALLOC(new_font_cfg.FontDataSize);
2499 new_font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas = true;
2500 memcpy(new_font_cfg.FontData, font_cfg->FontData, (size_t)new_font_cfg.FontDataSize);
2501 }
2502
2503 if (new_font_cfg.DstFont->EllipsisChar == (ImWchar)-1)
2504 new_font_cfg.DstFont->EllipsisChar = font_cfg->EllipsisChar;
2505
2506 ImFontAtlasUpdateConfigDataPointers(this);
2507
2508 // Invalidate texture
2509 TexReady = false;
2510 ClearTexData();
2511 return new_font_cfg.DstFont;
2512}
2513
2514// Default font TTF is compressed with stb_compress then base85 encoded (see misc/fonts/binary_to_compressed_c.cpp for encoder)
2515static unsigned int stb_decompress_length(const unsigned char* input);
2516static unsigned int stb_decompress(unsigned char* output, const unsigned char* input, unsigned int length);
2517static const char* GetDefaultCompressedFontDataTTFBase85();
2518static unsigned int Decode85Byte(char c) { return c >= '\\' ? c-36 : c-35; }
2519static void Decode85(const unsigned char* src, unsigned char* dst)
2520{
2521 while (*src)
2522 {
2523 unsigned int tmp = Decode85Byte(src[0]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[1]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[2]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[3]) + 85 * Decode85Byte(src[4]))));
2524 dst[0] = ((tmp >> 0) & 0xFF); dst[1] = ((tmp >> 8) & 0xFF); dst[2] = ((tmp >> 16) & 0xFF); dst[3] = ((tmp >> 24) & 0xFF); // We can't assume little-endianness.
2525 src += 5;
2526 dst += 4;
2527 }
2528}
2529
2530// Load embedded ProggyClean.ttf at size 13, disable oversampling
2531ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontDefault(const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template)
2532{
2533 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2534 if (!font_cfg_template)
2535 {
2536 font_cfg.OversampleH = font_cfg.OversampleV = 1;
2537 font_cfg.PixelSnapH = true;
2538 }
2539 if (font_cfg.SizePixels <= 0.0f)
2540 font_cfg.SizePixels = 13.0f * 1.0f;
2541 if (font_cfg.Name[0] == '\0')
2542 ImFormatString(font_cfg.Name, IM_ARRAYSIZE(font_cfg.Name), "ProggyClean.ttf, %dpx", (int)font_cfg.SizePixels);
2543 font_cfg.EllipsisChar = (ImWchar)0x0085;
2544 font_cfg.GlyphOffset.y = 1.0f * IM_TRUNC(font_cfg.SizePixels / 13.0f); // Add +1 offset per 13 units
2545
2546 const char* ttf_compressed_base85 = GetDefaultCompressedFontDataTTFBase85();
2547 const ImWchar* glyph_ranges = font_cfg.GlyphRanges != NULL ? font_cfg.GlyphRanges : GetGlyphRangesDefault();
2548 ImFont* font = AddFontFromMemoryCompressedBase85TTF(ttf_compressed_base85, font_cfg.SizePixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2549 return font;
2550}
2551
2552ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromFileTTF(const char* filename, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2553{
2554 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2555 size_t data_size = 0;
2556 void* data = ImFileLoadToMemory(filename, "rb", &data_size, 0);
2557 if (!data)
2558 {
2559 IM_ASSERT_USER_ERROR(0, "Could not load font file!");
2560 return NULL;
2561 }
2562 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2563 if (font_cfg.Name[0] == '\0')
2564 {
2565 // Store a short copy of filename into into the font name for convenience
2566 const char* p;
2567 for (p = filename + strlen(filename); p > filename && p[-1] != '/' && p[-1] != '\\'; p--) {}
2568 ImFormatString(font_cfg.Name, IM_ARRAYSIZE(font_cfg.Name), "%s, %.0fpx", p, size_pixels);
2569 }
2570 return AddFontFromMemoryTTF(data, (int)data_size, size_pixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2571}
2572
2573// NB: Transfer ownership of 'ttf_data' to ImFontAtlas, unless font_cfg_template->FontDataOwnedByAtlas == false. Owned TTF buffer will be deleted after Build().
2574ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryTTF(void* font_data, int font_data_size, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2575{
2576 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2577 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2578 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg.FontData == NULL);
2579 IM_ASSERT(font_data_size > 100 && "Incorrect value for font_data_size!"); // Heuristic to prevent accidentally passing a wrong value to font_data_size.
2580 font_cfg.FontData = font_data;
2581 font_cfg.FontDataSize = font_data_size;
2582 font_cfg.SizePixels = size_pixels > 0.0f ? size_pixels : font_cfg.SizePixels;
2583 if (glyph_ranges)
2584 font_cfg.GlyphRanges = glyph_ranges;
2585 return AddFont(&font_cfg);
2586}
2587
2588ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(const void* compressed_ttf_data, int compressed_ttf_size, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2589{
2590 const unsigned int buf_decompressed_size = stb_decompress_length((const unsigned char*)compressed_ttf_data);
2591 unsigned char* buf_decompressed_data = (unsigned char*)IM_ALLOC(buf_decompressed_size);
2592 stb_decompress(buf_decompressed_data, (const unsigned char*)compressed_ttf_data, (unsigned int)compressed_ttf_size);
2593
2594 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2595 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg.FontData == NULL);
2596 font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas = true;
2597 return AddFontFromMemoryTTF(buf_decompressed_data, (int)buf_decompressed_size, size_pixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2598}
2599
2600ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryCompressedBase85TTF(const char* compressed_ttf_data_base85, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2601{
2602 int compressed_ttf_size = (((int)strlen(compressed_ttf_data_base85) + 4) / 5) * 4;
2603 void* compressed_ttf = IM_ALLOC((size_t)compressed_ttf_size);
2604 Decode85((const unsigned char*)compressed_ttf_data_base85, (unsigned char*)compressed_ttf);
2605 ImFont* font = AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(compressed_ttf, compressed_ttf_size, size_pixels, font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2606 IM_FREE(compressed_ttf);
2607 return font;
2608}
2609
2610int ImFontAtlas::AddCustomRectRegular(int width, int height)
2611{
2612 IM_ASSERT(width > 0 && width <= 0xFFFF);
2613 IM_ASSERT(height > 0 && height <= 0xFFFF);
2614 ImFontAtlasCustomRect r;
2615 r.Width = (unsigned short)width;
2616 r.Height = (unsigned short)height;
2617 CustomRects.push_back(r);
2618 return CustomRects.Size - 1; // Return index
2619}
2620
2621int ImFontAtlas::AddCustomRectFontGlyph(ImFont* font, ImWchar id, int width, int height, float advance_x, const ImVec2& offset)
2622{
2623#ifdef IMGUI_USE_WCHAR32
2624 IM_ASSERT(id <= IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX);
2625#endif
2626 IM_ASSERT(font != NULL);
2627 IM_ASSERT(width > 0 && width <= 0xFFFF);
2628 IM_ASSERT(height > 0 && height <= 0xFFFF);
2629 ImFontAtlasCustomRect r;
2630 r.Width = (unsigned short)width;
2631 r.Height = (unsigned short)height;
2632 r.GlyphID = id;
2633 r.GlyphAdvanceX = advance_x;
2634 r.GlyphOffset = offset;
2635 r.Font = font;
2636 CustomRects.push_back(r);
2637 return CustomRects.Size - 1; // Return index
2638}
2639
2640void ImFontAtlas::CalcCustomRectUV(const ImFontAtlasCustomRect* rect, ImVec2* out_uv_min, ImVec2* out_uv_max) const
2641{
2642 IM_ASSERT(TexWidth > 0 && TexHeight > 0); // Font atlas needs to be built before we can calculate UV coordinates
2643 IM_ASSERT(rect->IsPacked()); // Make sure the rectangle has been packed
2644 *out_uv_min = ImVec2((float)rect->X * TexUvScale.x, (float)rect->Y * TexUvScale.y);
2645 *out_uv_max = ImVec2((float)(rect->X + rect->Width) * TexUvScale.x, (float)(rect->Y + rect->Height) * TexUvScale.y);
2646}
2647
2648bool ImFontAtlas::GetMouseCursorTexData(ImGuiMouseCursor cursor_type, ImVec2* out_offset, ImVec2* out_size, ImVec2 out_uv_border[2], ImVec2 out_uv_fill[2])
2649{
2650 if (cursor_type <= ImGuiMouseCursor_None || cursor_type >= ImGuiMouseCursor_COUNT)
2651 return false;
2652 if (Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors)
2653 return false;
2654
2655 IM_ASSERT(PackIdMouseCursors != -1);
2656 ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = GetCustomRectByIndex(PackIdMouseCursors);
2657 ImVec2 pos = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][0] + ImVec2((float)r->X, (float)r->Y);
2658 ImVec2 size = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][1];
2659 *out_size = size;
2660 *out_offset = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][2];
2661 out_uv_border[0] = (pos) * TexUvScale;
2662 out_uv_border[1] = (pos + size) * TexUvScale;
2663 pos.x += FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W + 1;
2664 out_uv_fill[0] = (pos) * TexUvScale;
2665 out_uv_fill[1] = (pos + size) * TexUvScale;
2666 return true;
2667}
2668
2669bool ImFontAtlas::Build()
2670{
2671 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2672
2673 // Default font is none are specified
2674 if (ConfigData.Size == 0)
2675 AddFontDefault();
2676
2677 // Select builder
2678 // - Note that we do not reassign to atlas->FontBuilderIO, since it is likely to point to static data which
2679 // may mess with some hot-reloading schemes. If you need to assign to this (for dynamic selection) AND are
2680 // using a hot-reloading scheme that messes up static data, store your own instance of ImFontBuilderIO somewhere
2681 // and point to it instead of pointing directly to return value of the GetBuilderXXX functions.
2682 const ImFontBuilderIO* builder_io = FontBuilderIO;
2683 if (builder_io == NULL)
2684 {
2685#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_FREETYPE
2686 builder_io = ImGuiFreeType::GetBuilderForFreeType();
2687#elif defined(IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE)
2688 builder_io = ImFontAtlasGetBuilderForStbTruetype();
2689#else
2690 IM_ASSERT(0); // Invalid Build function
2691#endif
2692 }
2693
2694 // Build
2695 return builder_io->FontBuilder_Build(this);
2696}
2697
2698void ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyCalcLookupTable(unsigned char out_table[256], float in_brighten_factor)
2699{
2700 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < 256; i++)
2701 {
2702 unsigned int value = (unsigned int)(i * in_brighten_factor);
2703 out_table[i] = value > 255 ? 255 : (value & 0xFF);
2704 }
2705}
2706
2707void ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyRectAlpha8(const unsigned char table[256], unsigned char* pixels, int x, int y, int w, int h, int stride)
2708{
2709 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(w <= stride);
2710 unsigned char* data = pixels + x + y * stride;
2711 for (int j = h; j > 0; j--, data += stride - w)
2712 for (int i = w; i > 0; i--, data++)
2713 *data = table[*data];
2714}
2715
2716#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
2717// Temporary data for one source font (multiple source fonts can be merged into one destination ImFont)
2718// (C++03 doesn't allow instancing ImVector<> with function-local types so we declare the type here.)
2719struct ImFontBuildSrcData
2720{
2721 stbtt_fontinfo FontInfo;
2722 stbtt_pack_range PackRange; // Hold the list of codepoints to pack (essentially points to Codepoints.Data)
2723 stbrp_rect* Rects; // Rectangle to pack. We first fill in their size and the packer will give us their position.
2724 stbtt_packedchar* PackedChars; // Output glyphs
2725 const ImWchar* SrcRanges; // Ranges as requested by user (user is allowed to request too much, e.g. 0x0020..0xFFFF)
2726 int DstIndex; // Index into atlas->Fonts[] and dst_tmp_array[]
2727 int GlyphsHighest; // Highest requested codepoint
2728 int GlyphsCount; // Glyph count (excluding missing glyphs and glyphs already set by an earlier source font)
2729 ImBitVector GlyphsSet; // Glyph bit map (random access, 1-bit per codepoint. This will be a maximum of 8KB)
2730 ImVector<int> GlyphsList; // Glyph codepoints list (flattened version of GlyphsSet)
2731};
2732
2733// Temporary data for one destination ImFont* (multiple source fonts can be merged into one destination ImFont)
2734struct ImFontBuildDstData
2735{
2736 int SrcCount; // Number of source fonts targeting this destination font.
2737 int GlyphsHighest;
2738 int GlyphsCount;
2739 ImBitVector GlyphsSet; // This is used to resolve collision when multiple sources are merged into a same destination font.
2740};
2741
2742static void UnpackBitVectorToFlatIndexList(const ImBitVector* in, ImVector<int>* out)
2743{
2744 IM_ASSERT(sizeof(in->Storage.Data[0]) == sizeof(int));
2745 const ImU32* it_begin = in->Storage.begin();
2746 const ImU32* it_end = in->Storage.end();
2747 for (const ImU32* it = it_begin; it < it_end; it++)
2748 if (ImU32 entries_32 = *it)
2749 for (ImU32 bit_n = 0; bit_n < 32; bit_n++)
2750 if (entries_32 & ((ImU32)1 << bit_n))
2751 out->push_back((int)(((it - it_begin) << 5) + bit_n));
2752}
2753
2754static bool ImFontAtlasBuildWithStbTruetype(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
2755{
2756 IM_ASSERT(atlas->ConfigData.Size > 0);
2757
2758 ImFontAtlasBuildInit(atlas);
2759
2760 // Clear atlas
2761 atlas->TexID = (ImTextureID)NULL;
2762 atlas->TexWidth = atlas->TexHeight = 0;
2763 atlas->TexUvScale = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
2764 atlas->TexUvWhitePixel = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
2765 atlas->ClearTexData();
2766
2767 // Temporary storage for building
2768 ImVector<ImFontBuildSrcData> src_tmp_array;
2769 ImVector<ImFontBuildDstData> dst_tmp_array;
2770 src_tmp_array.resize(atlas->ConfigData.Size);
2771 dst_tmp_array.resize(atlas->Fonts.Size);
2772 memset(src_tmp_array.Data, 0, (size_t)src_tmp_array.size_in_bytes());
2773 memset(dst_tmp_array.Data, 0, (size_t)dst_tmp_array.size_in_bytes());
2774
2775 // 1. Initialize font loading structure, check font data validity
2776 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < atlas->ConfigData.Size; src_i++)
2777 {
2778 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2779 ImFontConfig& cfg = atlas->ConfigData[src_i];
2780 IM_ASSERT(cfg.DstFont && (!cfg.DstFont->IsLoaded() || cfg.DstFont->ContainerAtlas == atlas));
2781
2782 // Find index from cfg.DstFont (we allow the user to set cfg.DstFont. Also it makes casual debugging nicer than when storing indices)
2783 src_tmp.DstIndex = -1;
2784 for (int output_i = 0; output_i < atlas->Fonts.Size && src_tmp.DstIndex == -1; output_i++)
2785 if (cfg.DstFont == atlas->Fonts[output_i])
2786 src_tmp.DstIndex = output_i;
2787 if (src_tmp.DstIndex == -1)
2788 {
2789 IM_ASSERT(src_tmp.DstIndex != -1); // cfg.DstFont not pointing within atlas->Fonts[] array?
2790 return false;
2791 }
2792 // Initialize helper structure for font loading and verify that the TTF/OTF data is correct
2793 const int font_offset = stbtt_GetFontOffsetForIndex((unsigned char*)cfg.FontData, cfg.FontNo);
2794 IM_ASSERT(font_offset >= 0 && "FontData is incorrect, or FontNo cannot be found.");
2795 if (!stbtt_InitFont(&src_tmp.FontInfo, (unsigned char*)cfg.FontData, font_offset))
2796 {
2797 IM_ASSERT(0 && "stbtt_InitFont(): failed to parse FontData. It is correct and complete? Check FontDataSize.");
2798 return false;
2799 }
2800
2801 // Measure highest codepoints
2802 ImFontBuildDstData& dst_tmp = dst_tmp_array[src_tmp.DstIndex];
2803 src_tmp.SrcRanges = cfg.GlyphRanges ? cfg.GlyphRanges : atlas->GetGlyphRangesDefault();
2804 for (const ImWchar* src_range = src_tmp.SrcRanges; src_range[0] && src_range[1]; src_range += 2)
2805 {
2806 // Check for valid range. This may also help detect *some* dangling pointers, because a common
2807 // user error is to setup ImFontConfig::GlyphRanges with a pointer to data that isn't persistent.
2808 IM_ASSERT(src_range[0] <= src_range[1]);
2809 src_tmp.GlyphsHighest = ImMax(src_tmp.GlyphsHighest, (int)src_range[1]);
2810 }
2811 dst_tmp.SrcCount++;
2812 dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest = ImMax(dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest, src_tmp.GlyphsHighest);
2813 }
2814
2815 // 2. For every requested codepoint, check for their presence in the font data, and handle redundancy or overlaps between source fonts to avoid unused glyphs.
2816 int total_glyphs_count = 0;
2817 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2818 {
2819 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2820 ImFontBuildDstData& dst_tmp = dst_tmp_array[src_tmp.DstIndex];
2821 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.Create(src_tmp.GlyphsHighest + 1);
2822 if (dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.Storage.empty())
2823 dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.Create(dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest + 1);
2824
2825 for (const ImWchar* src_range = src_tmp.SrcRanges; src_range[0] && src_range[1]; src_range += 2)
2826 for (unsigned int codepoint = src_range[0]; codepoint <= src_range[1]; codepoint++)
2827 {
2828 if (dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.TestBit(codepoint)) // Don't overwrite existing glyphs. We could make this an option for MergeMode (e.g. MergeOverwrite==true)
2829 continue;
2830 if (!stbtt_FindGlyphIndex(&src_tmp.FontInfo, codepoint)) // It is actually in the font?
2831 continue;
2832
2833 // Add to avail set/counters
2834 src_tmp.GlyphsCount++;
2835 dst_tmp.GlyphsCount++;
2836 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);
2837 dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);
2838 total_glyphs_count++;
2839 }
2840 }
2841
2842 // 3. Unpack our bit map into a flat list (we now have all the Unicode points that we know are requested _and_ available _and_ not overlapping another)
2843 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2844 {
2845 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2846 src_tmp.GlyphsList.reserve(src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
2847 UnpackBitVectorToFlatIndexList(&src_tmp.GlyphsSet, &src_tmp.GlyphsList);
2848 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.Clear();
2849 IM_ASSERT(src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size == src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
2850 }
2851 for (int dst_i = 0; dst_i < dst_tmp_array.Size; dst_i++)
2852 dst_tmp_array[dst_i].GlyphsSet.Clear();
2853 dst_tmp_array.clear();
2854
2855 // Allocate packing character data and flag packed characters buffer as non-packed (x0=y0=x1=y1=0)
2856 // (We technically don't need to zero-clear buf_rects, but let's do it for the sake of sanity)
2857 ImVector<stbrp_rect> buf_rects;
2858 ImVector<stbtt_packedchar> buf_packedchars;
2859 buf_rects.resize(total_glyphs_count);
2860 buf_packedchars.resize(total_glyphs_count);
2861 memset(buf_rects.Data, 0, (size_t)buf_rects.size_in_bytes());
2862 memset(buf_packedchars.Data, 0, (size_t)buf_packedchars.size_in_bytes());
2863
2864 // 4. Gather glyphs sizes so we can pack them in our virtual canvas.
2865 int total_surface = 0;
2866 int buf_rects_out_n = 0;
2867 int buf_packedchars_out_n = 0;
2868 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2869 {
2870 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2871 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
2872 continue;
2873
2874 src_tmp.Rects = &buf_rects[buf_rects_out_n];
2875 src_tmp.PackedChars = &buf_packedchars[buf_packedchars_out_n];
2876 buf_rects_out_n += src_tmp.GlyphsCount;
2877 buf_packedchars_out_n += src_tmp.GlyphsCount;
2878
2879 // Convert our ranges in the format stb_truetype wants
2880 ImFontConfig& cfg = atlas->ConfigData[src_i];
2881 src_tmp.PackRange.font_size = cfg.SizePixels * cfg.RasterizerDensity;
2882 src_tmp.PackRange.first_unicode_codepoint_in_range = 0;
2883 src_tmp.PackRange.array_of_unicode_codepoints = src_tmp.GlyphsList.Data;
2884 src_tmp.PackRange.num_chars = src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size;
2885 src_tmp.PackRange.chardata_for_range = src_tmp.PackedChars;
2886 src_tmp.PackRange.h_oversample = (unsigned char)cfg.OversampleH;
2887 src_tmp.PackRange.v_oversample = (unsigned char)cfg.OversampleV;
2888
2889 // Gather the sizes of all rectangles we will need to pack (this loop is based on stbtt_PackFontRangesGatherRects)
2890 const float scale = (cfg.SizePixels > 0.0f) ? stbtt_ScaleForPixelHeight(&src_tmp.FontInfo, cfg.SizePixels * cfg.RasterizerDensity) : stbtt_ScaleForMappingEmToPixels(&src_tmp.FontInfo, -cfg.SizePixels * cfg.RasterizerDensity);
2891 const int padding = atlas->TexGlyphPadding;
2892 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size; glyph_i++)
2893 {
2894 int x0, y0, x1, y1;
2895 const int glyph_index_in_font = stbtt_FindGlyphIndex(&src_tmp.FontInfo, src_tmp.GlyphsList[glyph_i]);
2896 IM_ASSERT(glyph_index_in_font != 0);
2897 stbtt_GetGlyphBitmapBoxSubpixel(&src_tmp.FontInfo, glyph_index_in_font, scale * cfg.OversampleH, scale * cfg.OversampleV, 0, 0, &x0, &y0, &x1, &y1);
2898 src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].w = (stbrp_coord)(x1 - x0 + padding + cfg.OversampleH - 1);
2899 src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h = (stbrp_coord)(y1 - y0 + padding + cfg.OversampleV - 1);
2900 total_surface += src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].w * src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h;
2901 }
2902 }
2903
2904 // We need a width for the skyline algorithm, any width!
2905 // The exact width doesn't really matter much, but some API/GPU have texture size limitations and increasing width can decrease height.
2906 // User can override TexDesiredWidth and TexGlyphPadding if they wish, otherwise we use a simple heuristic to select the width based on expected surface.
2907 const int surface_sqrt = (int)ImSqrt((float)total_surface) + 1;
2908 atlas->TexHeight = 0;
2909 if (atlas->TexDesiredWidth > 0)
2910 atlas->TexWidth = atlas->TexDesiredWidth;
2911 else
2912 atlas->TexWidth = (surface_sqrt >= 4096 * 0.7f) ? 4096 : (surface_sqrt >= 2048 * 0.7f) ? 2048 : (surface_sqrt >= 1024 * 0.7f) ? 1024 : 512;
2913
2914 // 5. Start packing
2915 // Pack our extra data rectangles first, so it will be on the upper-left corner of our texture (UV will have small values).
2916 const int TEX_HEIGHT_MAX = 1024 * 32;
2917 stbtt_pack_context spc = {};
2918 stbtt_PackBegin(&spc, NULL, atlas->TexWidth, TEX_HEIGHT_MAX, 0, atlas->TexGlyphPadding, NULL);
2919 ImFontAtlasBuildPackCustomRects(atlas, spc.pack_info);
2920
2921 // 6. Pack each source font. No rendering yet, we are working with rectangles in an infinitely tall texture at this point.
2922 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2923 {
2924 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2925 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
2926 continue;
2927
2928 stbrp_pack_rects((stbrp_context*)spc.pack_info, src_tmp.Rects, src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
2929
2930 // Extend texture height and mark missing glyphs as non-packed so we won't render them.
2931 // FIXME: We are not handling packing failure here (would happen if we got off TEX_HEIGHT_MAX or if a single if larger than TexWidth?)
2932 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++)
2933 if (src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].was_packed)
2934 atlas->TexHeight = ImMax(atlas->TexHeight, src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].y + src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h);
2935 }
2936
2937 // 7. Allocate texture
2938 atlas->TexHeight = (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoPowerOfTwoHeight) ? (atlas->TexHeight + 1) : ImUpperPowerOfTwo(atlas->TexHeight);
2939 atlas->TexUvScale = ImVec2(1.0f / atlas->TexWidth, 1.0f / atlas->TexHeight);
2940 atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 = (unsigned char*)IM_ALLOC(atlas->TexWidth * atlas->TexHeight);
2941 memset(atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8, 0, atlas->TexWidth * atlas->TexHeight);
2942 spc.pixels = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8;
2943 spc.height = atlas->TexHeight;
2944
2945 // 8. Render/rasterize font characters into the texture
2946 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2947 {
2948 ImFontConfig& cfg = atlas->ConfigData[src_i];
2949 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2950 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
2951 continue;
2952
2953 stbtt_PackFontRangesRenderIntoRects(&spc, &src_tmp.FontInfo, &src_tmp.PackRange, 1, src_tmp.Rects);
2954
2955 // Apply multiply operator
2956 if (cfg.RasterizerMultiply != 1.0f)
2957 {
2958 unsigned char multiply_table[256];
2959 ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyCalcLookupTable(multiply_table, cfg.RasterizerMultiply);
2960 stbrp_rect* r = &src_tmp.Rects[0];
2961 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++, r++)
2962 if (r->was_packed)
2963 ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyRectAlpha8(multiply_table, atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8, r->x, r->y, r->w, r->h, atlas->TexWidth * 1);
2964 }
2965 src_tmp.Rects = NULL;
2966 }
2967
2968 // End packing
2969 stbtt_PackEnd(&spc);
2970 buf_rects.clear();
2971
2972 // 9. Setup ImFont and glyphs for runtime
2973 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2974 {
2975 // When merging fonts with MergeMode=true:
2976 // - We can have multiple input fonts writing into a same destination font.
2977 // - dst_font->ConfigData is != from cfg which is our source configuration.
2978 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2979 ImFontConfig& cfg = atlas->ConfigData[src_i];
2980 ImFont* dst_font = cfg.DstFont;
2981
2982 const float font_scale = stbtt_ScaleForPixelHeight(&src_tmp.FontInfo, cfg.SizePixels);
2983 int unscaled_ascent, unscaled_descent, unscaled_line_gap;
2984 stbtt_GetFontVMetrics(&src_tmp.FontInfo, &unscaled_ascent, &unscaled_descent, &unscaled_line_gap);
2985
2986 const float ascent = ImTrunc(unscaled_ascent * font_scale + ((unscaled_ascent > 0.0f) ? +1 : -1));
2987 const float descent = ImTrunc(unscaled_descent * font_scale + ((unscaled_descent > 0.0f) ? +1 : -1));
2988 ImFontAtlasBuildSetupFont(atlas, dst_font, &cfg, ascent, descent);
2989 const float font_off_x = cfg.GlyphOffset.x;
2990 const float font_off_y = cfg.GlyphOffset.y + IM_ROUND(dst_font->Ascent);
2991
2992 const float inv_rasterization_scale = 1.0f / cfg.RasterizerDensity;
2993
2994 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++)
2995 {
2996 // Register glyph
2997 const int codepoint = src_tmp.GlyphsList[glyph_i];
2998 const stbtt_packedchar& pc = src_tmp.PackedChars[glyph_i];
2999 stbtt_aligned_quad q;
3000 float unused_x = 0.0f, unused_y = 0.0f;
3001 stbtt_GetPackedQuad(src_tmp.PackedChars, atlas->TexWidth, atlas->TexHeight, glyph_i, &unused_x, &unused_y, &q, 0);
3002 float x0 = q.x0 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_x;
3003 float y0 = q.y0 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_y;
3004 float x1 = q.x1 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_x;
3005 float y1 = q.y1 * inv_rasterization_scale + font_off_y;
3006 dst_font->AddGlyph(&cfg, (ImWchar)codepoint, x0, y0, x1, y1, q.s0, q.t0, q.s1, q.t1, pc.xadvance * inv_rasterization_scale);
3007 }
3008 }
3009
3010 // Cleanup
3011 src_tmp_array.clear_destruct();
3012
3013 ImFontAtlasBuildFinish(atlas);
3014 return true;
3015}

3052
3053void ImFontAtlasBuildPackCustomRects(ImFontAtlas* atlas, void* stbrp_context_opaque)
3054{
3055 stbrp_context* pack_context = (stbrp_context*)stbrp_context_opaque;
3056 IM_ASSERT(pack_context != NULL);
3057
3058 ImVector<ImFontAtlasCustomRect>& user_rects = atlas->CustomRects;
3059 IM_ASSERT(user_rects.Size >= 1); // We expect at least the default custom rects to be registered, else something went wrong.
3060#ifdef __GNUC__
3061 if (user_rects.Size < 1) { __builtin_unreachable(); } // Workaround for GCC bug if IM_ASSERT() is defined to conditionally throw (see #5343)
3062#endif
3063
3064 ImVector<stbrp_rect> pack_rects;
3065 pack_rects.resize(user_rects.Size);
3066 memset(pack_rects.Data, 0, (size_t)pack_rects.size_in_bytes());
3067 for (int i = 0; i < user_rects.Size; i++)
3068 {
3069 pack_rects[i].w = user_rects[i].Width;
3070 pack_rects[i].h = user_rects[i].Height;
3071 }
3072 stbrp_pack_rects(pack_context, &pack_rects[0], pack_rects.Size);
3073 for (int i = 0; i < pack_rects.Size; i++)
3074 if (pack_rects[i].was_packed)
3075 {
3076 user_rects[i].X = (unsigned short)pack_rects[i].x;
3077 user_rects[i].Y = (unsigned short)pack_rects[i].y;
3078 IM_ASSERT(pack_rects[i].w == user_rects[i].Width && pack_rects[i].h == user_rects[i].Height);
3079 atlas->TexHeight = ImMax(atlas->TexHeight, pack_rects[i].y + pack_rects[i].h);
3080 }
3081}
3082
3083void ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(ImFontAtlas* atlas, int x, int y, int w, int h, const char* in_str, char in_marker_char, unsigned char in_marker_pixel_value)
3084{
3085 IM_ASSERT(x >= 0 && x + w <= atlas->TexWidth);
3086 IM_ASSERT(y >= 0 && y + h <= atlas->TexHeight);
3087 unsigned char* out_pixel = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 + x + (y * atlas->TexWidth);
3088 for (int off_y = 0; off_y < h; off_y++, out_pixel += atlas->TexWidth, in_str += w)
3089 for (int off_x = 0; off_x < w; off_x++)
3090 out_pixel[off_x] = (in_str[off_x] == in_marker_char) ? in_marker_pixel_value : 0x00;
3091}
3092
3093void ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(ImFontAtlas* atlas, int x, int y, int w, int h, const char* in_str, char in_marker_char, unsigned int in_marker_pixel_value)
3094{
3095 IM_ASSERT(x >= 0 && x + w <= atlas->TexWidth);
3096 IM_ASSERT(y >= 0 && y + h <= atlas->TexHeight);
3097 unsigned int* out_pixel = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32 + x + (y * atlas->TexWidth);
3098 for (int off_y = 0; off_y < h; off_y++, out_pixel += atlas->TexWidth, in_str += w)
3099 for (int off_x = 0; off_x < w; off_x++)
3100 out_pixel[off_x] = (in_str[off_x] == in_marker_char) ? in_marker_pixel_value : IM_COL32_BLACK_TRANS;
3101}
3102
3103static void ImFontAtlasBuildRenderDefaultTexData(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
3104{
3105 ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdMouseCursors);
3106 IM_ASSERT(r->IsPacked());
3107
3108 const int w = atlas->TexWidth;
3109 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors))
3110 {
3111 // Render/copy pixels
3112 IM_ASSERT(r->Width == FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W * 2 + 1 && r->Height == FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H);
3113 const int x_for_white = r->X;
3114 const int x_for_black = r->X + FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W + 1;
3115 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
3116 {
3117 ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_white, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, '.', 0xFF);
3118 ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_black, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, 'X', 0xFF);
3119 }
3120 else
3121 {
3122 ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_white, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, '.', IM_COL32_WHITE);
3123 ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_black, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, 'X', IM_COL32_WHITE);
3124 }
3125 }
3126 else
3127 {
3128 // Render 4 white pixels
3129 IM_ASSERT(r->Width == 2 && r->Height == 2);
3130 const int offset = (int)r->X + (int)r->Y * w;
3131 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
3132 {
3133 atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + 1] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + w] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + w + 1] = 0xFF;
3134 }
3135 else
3136 {
3137 atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + 1] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + w] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + w + 1] = IM_COL32_WHITE;
3138 }
3139 }
3140 atlas->TexUvWhitePixel = ImVec2((r->X + 0.5f) * atlas->TexUvScale.x, (r->Y + 0.5f) * atlas->TexUvScale.y);
3141}
3142
3143static void ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
3144{
3145 if (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines)
3146 return;
3147
3148 // This generates a triangular shape in the texture, with the various line widths stacked on top of each other to allow interpolation between them
3149 ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdLines);
3150 IM_ASSERT(r->IsPacked());
3151 for (unsigned int n = 0; n < IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 1; n++) // +1 because of the zero-width row
3152 {
3153 // Each line consists of at least two empty pixels at the ends, with a line of solid pixels in the middle
3154 unsigned int y = n;
3155 unsigned int line_width = n;
3156 unsigned int pad_left = (r->Width - line_width) / 2;
3157 unsigned int pad_right = r->Width - (pad_left + line_width);
3158
3159 // Write each slice
3160 IM_ASSERT(pad_left + line_width + pad_right == r->Width && y < r->Height); // Make sure we're inside the texture bounds before we start writing pixels
3161 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
3162 {
3163 unsigned char* write_ptr = &atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[r->X + ((r->Y + y) * atlas->TexWidth)];
3164 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < pad_left; i++)
3165 *(write_ptr + i) = 0x00;
3166
3167 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < line_width; i++)
3168 *(write_ptr + pad_left + i) = 0xFF;
3169
3170 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < pad_right; i++)
3171 *(write_ptr + pad_left + line_width + i) = 0x00;
3172 }
3173 else
3174 {
3175 unsigned int* write_ptr = &atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[r->X + ((r->Y + y) * atlas->TexWidth)];
3176 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < pad_left; i++)
3177 *(write_ptr + i) = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, 0);
3178
3179 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < line_width; i++)
3180 *(write_ptr + pad_left + i) = IM_COL32_WHITE;
3181
3182 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < pad_right; i++)
3183 *(write_ptr + pad_left + line_width + i) = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, 0);
3184 }
3185
3186 // Calculate UVs for this line
3187 ImVec2 uv0 = ImVec2((float)(r->X + pad_left - 1), (float)(r->Y + y)) * atlas->TexUvScale;
3188 ImVec2 uv1 = ImVec2((float)(r->X + pad_left + line_width + 1), (float)(r->Y + y + 1)) * atlas->TexUvScale;
3189 float half_v = (uv0.y + uv1.y) * 0.5f; // Calculate a constant V in the middle of the row to avoid sampling artifacts
3190 atlas->TexUvLines[n] = ImVec4(uv0.x, half_v, uv1.x, half_v);
3191 }
3192}
3193
3194// Note: this is called / shared by both the stb_truetype and the FreeType builder
3195void ImFontAtlasBuildInit(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
3196{
3197 // Round font size
3198 // - We started rounding in 1.90 WIP (18991) as our layout system currently doesn't support non-rounded font size well yet.
3199 // - Note that using io.FontGlobalScale or SetWindowFontScale(), with are legacy-ish, partially supported features, can still lead to unrounded sizes.
3200 // - We may support it better later and remove this rounding.
3201 for (ImFontConfig& cfg : atlas->ConfigData)
3202 cfg.SizePixels = ImTrunc(cfg.SizePixels);
3203
3204 // Register texture region for mouse cursors or standard white pixels
3205 if (atlas->PackIdMouseCursors < 0)
3206 {
3207 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors))
3208 atlas->PackIdMouseCursors = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W * 2 + 1, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H);
3209 else
3210 atlas->PackIdMouseCursors = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(2, 2);
3211 }
3212
3213 // Register texture region for thick lines
3214 // The +2 here is to give space for the end caps, whilst height +1 is to accommodate the fact we have a zero-width row
3215 if (atlas->PackIdLines < 0)
3216 {
3217 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines))
3218 atlas->PackIdLines = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 2, IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 1);
3219 }
3220}
3221
3222// This is called/shared by both the stb_truetype and the FreeType builder.
3223void ImFontAtlasBuildFinish(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
3224{
3225 // Render into our custom data blocks
3226 IM_ASSERT(atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL || atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32 != NULL);
3227 ImFontAtlasBuildRenderDefaultTexData(atlas);
3228 ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData(atlas);
3229
3230 // Register custom rectangle glyphs
3231 for (int i = 0; i < atlas->CustomRects.Size; i++)
3232 {
3233 const ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = &atlas->CustomRects[i];
3234 if (r->Font == NULL || r->GlyphID == 0)
3235 continue;
3236
3237 // Will ignore ImFontConfig settings: GlyphMinAdvanceX, GlyphMinAdvanceY, GlyphExtraSpacing, PixelSnapH
3238 IM_ASSERT(r->Font->ContainerAtlas == atlas);
3239 ImVec2 uv0, uv1;
3240 atlas->CalcCustomRectUV(r, &uv0, &uv1);
3241 r->Font->AddGlyph(NULL, (ImWchar)r->GlyphID, r->GlyphOffset.x, r->GlyphOffset.y, r->GlyphOffset.x + r->Width, r->GlyphOffset.y + r->Height, uv0.x, uv0.y, uv1.x, uv1.y, r->GlyphAdvanceX);
3242 }
3243
3244 // Build all fonts lookup tables
3245 for (ImFont* font : atlas->Fonts)
3246 if (font->DirtyLookupTables)
3247 font->BuildLookupTable();
3248
3249 atlas->TexReady = true;
3250}

3302
3303static void UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(int base_codepoint, const short* accumulative_offsets, int accumulative_offsets_count, ImWchar* out_ranges)
3304{
3305 for (int n = 0; n < accumulative_offsets_count; n++, out_ranges += 2)
3306 {
3307 out_ranges[0] = out_ranges[1] = (ImWchar)(base_codepoint + accumulative_offsets[n]);
3308 base_codepoint += accumulative_offsets[n];
3309 }
3310 out_ranges[0] = 0;
3311}

3376 static ImWchar full_ranges[IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges) + IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00) * 2 + 1] = { 0 };
3377 if (!full_ranges[0])
3378 {
3379 memcpy(full_ranges, base_ranges, sizeof(base_ranges));

3383}

3456 3,2,1,1,1,1,2,1,1,
3457 };
3458 static ImWchar base_ranges[] = // not zero-terminated
3459 {
3460 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3461 0x3000, 0x30FF, // CJK Symbols and Punctuations, Hiragana, Katakana
3462 0x31F0, 0x31FF, // Katakana Phonetic Extensions
3463 0xFF00, 0xFFEF, // Half-width characters
3464 0xFFFD, 0xFFFD // Invalid
3465 };
3466 static ImWchar full_ranges[IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges) + IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00)*2 + 1] = { 0 };
3467 if (!full_ranges[0])
3468 {
3469 memcpy(full_ranges, base_ranges, sizeof(base_ranges));
3470 UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(0x4E00, accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00, IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00), full_ranges + IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges));
3471 }
3472 return &full_ranges[0];
3473}

3517//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3518// [SECTION] ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder
3519//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3520
3521void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::AddText(const char* text, const char* text_end)
3522{
3523 while (text_end ? (text < text_end) : *text)
3524 {
3525 unsigned int c = 0;
3526 int c_len = ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, text, text_end);
3527 text += c_len;
3528 if (c_len == 0)
3529 break;
3530 AddChar((ImWchar)c);
3531 }
3532}
3533
3534void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::AddRanges(const ImWchar* ranges)
3535{
3536 for (; ranges[0]; ranges += 2)
3537 for (unsigned int c = ranges[0]; c <= ranges[1] && c <= IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX; c++) //-V560
3538 AddChar((ImWchar)c);
3539}
3540
3541void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::BuildRanges(ImVector<ImWchar>* out_ranges)
3542{
3543 const int max_codepoint = IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX;
3544 for (int n = 0; n <= max_codepoint; n++)
3545 if (GetBit(n))
3546 {
3547 out_ranges->push_back((ImWchar)n);
3548 while (n < max_codepoint && GetBit(n + 1))
3549 n++;
3550 out_ranges->push_back((ImWchar)n);
3551 }
3552 out_ranges->push_back(0);
3553}
