3555//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3556// [SECTION] ImFont
3557//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3558
3559ImFont::ImFont()
3560{
3561 FontSize = 0.0f;
3562 FallbackAdvanceX = 0.0f;
3563 FallbackChar = (ImWchar)-1;
3564 EllipsisChar = (ImWchar)-1;
3565 EllipsisWidth = EllipsisCharStep = 0.0f;
3566 EllipsisCharCount = 0;
3567 FallbackGlyph = NULL;
3568 ContainerAtlas = NULL;
3569 ConfigData = NULL;
3570 ConfigDataCount = 0;
3571 DirtyLookupTables = false;
3572 Scale = 1.0f;
3573 Ascent = Descent = 0.0f;
3574 MetricsTotalSurface = 0;
3575 memset(Used4kPagesMap, 0, sizeof(Used4kPagesMap));
3576}
3577
3578ImFont::~ImFont()
3579{
3580 ClearOutputData();
3581}
3582
3583void ImFont::ClearOutputData()
3584{
3585 FontSize = 0.0f;
3586 FallbackAdvanceX = 0.0f;
3587 Glyphs.clear();
3588 IndexAdvanceX.clear();
3589 IndexLookup.clear();
3590 FallbackGlyph = NULL;
3591 ContainerAtlas = NULL;
3592 DirtyLookupTables = true;
3593 Ascent = Descent = 0.0f;
3594 MetricsTotalSurface = 0;
3595}
3596
3597static ImWchar FindFirstExistingGlyph(ImFont* font, const ImWchar* candidate_chars, int candidate_chars_count)
3598{
3599 for (int n = 0; n < candidate_chars_count; n++)
3600 if (font->FindGlyphNoFallback(candidate_chars[n]) != NULL)
3601 return candidate_chars[n];
3602 return (ImWchar)-1;
3603}
3604
3605void ImFont::BuildLookupTable()
3606{
3607 int max_codepoint = 0;
3608 for (int i = 0; i != Glyphs.Size; i++)
3609 max_codepoint = ImMax(max_codepoint, (int)Glyphs[i].Codepoint);
3610
3611 // Build lookup table
3612 IM_ASSERT(Glyphs.Size > 0 && "Font has not loaded glyph!");
3613 IM_ASSERT(Glyphs.Size < 0xFFFF); // -1 is reserved
3614 IndexAdvanceX.clear();
3615 IndexLookup.clear();
3616 DirtyLookupTables = false;
3617 memset(Used4kPagesMap, 0, sizeof(Used4kPagesMap));
3618 GrowIndex(max_codepoint + 1);
3619 for (int i = 0; i < Glyphs.Size; i++)
3620 {
3621 int codepoint = (int)Glyphs[i].Codepoint;
3622 IndexAdvanceX[codepoint] = Glyphs[i].AdvanceX;
3623 IndexLookup[codepoint] = (ImWchar)i;
3624
3625 // Mark 4K page as used
3626 const int page_n = codepoint / 4096;
3627 Used4kPagesMap[page_n >> 3] |= 1 << (page_n & 7);
3628 }
3629
3630 // Create a glyph to handle TAB
3631 // FIXME: Needs proper TAB handling but it needs to be contextualized (or we could arbitrary say that each string starts at "column 0" ?)
3632 if (FindGlyph((ImWchar)' '))
3633 {
3634 if (Glyphs.back().Codepoint != '\t') // So we can call this function multiple times (FIXME: Flaky)
3635 Glyphs.resize(Glyphs.Size + 1);
3636 ImFontGlyph& tab_glyph = Glyphs.back();
3637 tab_glyph = *FindGlyph((ImWchar)' ');
3638 tab_glyph.Codepoint = '\t';
3639 tab_glyph.AdvanceX *= IM_TABSIZE;
3640 IndexAdvanceX[(int)tab_glyph.Codepoint] = (float)tab_glyph.AdvanceX;
3641 IndexLookup[(int)tab_glyph.Codepoint] = (ImWchar)(Glyphs.Size - 1);
3642 }
3643
3644 // Mark special glyphs as not visible (note that AddGlyph already mark as non-visible glyphs with zero-size polygons)
3645 SetGlyphVisible((ImWchar)' ', false);
3646 SetGlyphVisible((ImWchar)'\t', false);
3647
3648 // Setup Fallback character
3649 const ImWchar fallback_chars[] = { (ImWchar)IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_INVALID, (ImWchar)'?', (ImWchar)' ' };
3650 FallbackGlyph = FindGlyphNoFallback(FallbackChar);
3651 if (FallbackGlyph == NULL)
3652 {
3653 FallbackChar = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, fallback_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(fallback_chars));
3654 FallbackGlyph = FindGlyphNoFallback(FallbackChar);
3655 if (FallbackGlyph == NULL)
3656 {
3657 FallbackGlyph = &Glyphs.back();
3658 FallbackChar = (ImWchar)FallbackGlyph->Codepoint;
3659 }
3660 }
3661 FallbackAdvanceX = FallbackGlyph->AdvanceX;
3662 for (int i = 0; i < max_codepoint + 1; i++)
3663 if (IndexAdvanceX[i] < 0.0f)
3664 IndexAdvanceX[i] = FallbackAdvanceX;
3665
3666 // Setup Ellipsis character. It is required for rendering elided text. We prefer using U+2026 (horizontal ellipsis).
3667 // However some old fonts may contain ellipsis at U+0085. Here we auto-detect most suitable ellipsis character.
3668 // FIXME: Note that 0x2026 is rarely included in our font ranges. Because of this we are more likely to use three individual dots.
3669 const ImWchar ellipsis_chars[] = { (ImWchar)0x2026, (ImWchar)0x0085 };
3670 const ImWchar dots_chars[] = { (ImWchar)'.', (ImWchar)0xFF0E };
3671 if (EllipsisChar == (ImWchar)-1)
3672 EllipsisChar = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, ellipsis_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(ellipsis_chars));
3673 const ImWchar dot_char = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, dots_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(dots_chars));
3674 if (EllipsisChar != (ImWchar)-1)
3675 {
3676 EllipsisCharCount = 1;
3677 EllipsisWidth = EllipsisCharStep = FindGlyph(EllipsisChar)->X1;
3678 }
3679 else if (dot_char != (ImWchar)-1)
3680 {
3681 const ImFontGlyph* glyph = FindGlyph(dot_char);
3682 EllipsisChar = dot_char;
3683 EllipsisCharCount = 3;
3684 EllipsisCharStep = (glyph->X1 - glyph->X0) + 1.0f;
3685 EllipsisWidth = EllipsisCharStep * 3.0f - 1.0f;
3686 }
3687}
3688
3689// API is designed this way to avoid exposing the 4K page size
3690// e.g. use with IsGlyphRangeUnused(0, 255)
3691bool ImFont::IsGlyphRangeUnused(unsigned int c_begin, unsigned int c_last)
3692{
3693 unsigned int page_begin = (c_begin / 4096);
3694 unsigned int page_last = (c_last / 4096);
3695 for (unsigned int page_n = page_begin; page_n <= page_last; page_n++)
3696 if ((page_n >> 3) < sizeof(Used4kPagesMap))
3697 if (Used4kPagesMap[page_n >> 3] & (1 << (page_n & 7)))
3698 return false;
3699 return true;
3700}
3701
3702void ImFont::SetGlyphVisible(ImWchar c, bool visible)
3703{
3704 if (ImFontGlyph* glyph = (ImFontGlyph*)(void*)FindGlyph((ImWchar)c))
3705 glyph->Visible = visible ? 1 : 0;
3706}
3707
3708void ImFont::GrowIndex(int new_size)
3709{
3710 IM_ASSERT(IndexAdvanceX.Size == IndexLookup.Size);
3711 if (new_size <= IndexLookup.Size)
3712 return;
3713 IndexAdvanceX.resize(new_size, -1.0f);
3714 IndexLookup.resize(new_size, (ImWchar)-1);
3715}
3716
3717// x0/y0/x1/y1 are offset from the character upper-left layout position, in pixels. Therefore x0/y0 are often fairly close to zero.
3718// Not to be mistaken with texture coordinates, which are held by u0/v0/u1/v1 in normalized format (0.0..1.0 on each texture axis).
3719// 'cfg' is not necessarily == 'this->ConfigData' because multiple source fonts+configs can be used to build one target font.
3720void ImFont::AddGlyph(const ImFontConfig* cfg, ImWchar codepoint, float x0, float y0, float x1, float y1, float u0, float v0, float u1, float v1, float advance_x)
3721{
3722 if (cfg != NULL)
3723 {
3724 // Clamp & recenter if needed
3725 const float advance_x_original = advance_x;
3726 advance_x = ImClamp(advance_x, cfg->GlyphMinAdvanceX, cfg->GlyphMaxAdvanceX);
3727 if (advance_x != advance_x_original)
3728 {
3729 float char_off_x = cfg->PixelSnapH ? ImTrunc((advance_x - advance_x_original) * 0.5f) : (advance_x - advance_x_original) * 0.5f;
3730 x0 += char_off_x;
3731 x1 += char_off_x;
3732 }
3733
3734 // Snap to pixel
3735 if (cfg->PixelSnapH)
3736 advance_x = IM_ROUND(advance_x);
3737
3738 // Bake spacing
3739 advance_x += cfg->GlyphExtraSpacing.x;
3740 }
3741
3742 Glyphs.resize(Glyphs.Size + 1);
3743 ImFontGlyph& glyph = Glyphs.back();
3744 glyph.Codepoint = (unsigned int)codepoint;
3745 glyph.Visible = (x0 != x1) && (y0 != y1);
3746 glyph.Colored = false;
3747 glyph.X0 = x0;
3748 glyph.Y0 = y0;
3749 glyph.X1 = x1;
3750 glyph.Y1 = y1;
3751 glyph.U0 = u0;
3752 glyph.V0 = v0;
3753 glyph.U1 = u1;
3754 glyph.V1 = v1;
3755 glyph.AdvanceX = advance_x;
3756
3757 // Compute rough surface usage metrics (+1 to account for average padding, +0.99 to round)
3758 // We use (U1-U0)*TexWidth instead of X1-X0 to account for oversampling.
3759 float pad = ContainerAtlas->TexGlyphPadding + 0.99f;
3760 DirtyLookupTables = true;
3761 MetricsTotalSurface += (int)((glyph.U1 - glyph.U0) * ContainerAtlas->TexWidth + pad) * (int)((glyph.V1 - glyph.V0) * ContainerAtlas->TexHeight + pad);
3762}
3763
3764void ImFont::AddRemapChar(ImWchar dst, ImWchar src, bool overwrite_dst)
3765{
3766 IM_ASSERT(IndexLookup.Size > 0); // Currently this can only be called AFTER the font has been built, aka after calling ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAs*() function.
3767 unsigned int index_size = (unsigned int)IndexLookup.Size;
3768
3769 if (dst < index_size && IndexLookup.Data[dst] == (ImWchar)-1 && !overwrite_dst) // 'dst' already exists
3770 return;
3771 if (src >= index_size && dst >= index_size) // both 'dst' and 'src' don't exist -> no-op
3772 return;
3773
3774 GrowIndex(dst + 1);
3775 IndexLookup[dst] = (src < index_size) ? IndexLookup.Data[src] : (ImWchar)-1;
3776 IndexAdvanceX[dst] = (src < index_size) ? IndexAdvanceX.Data[src] : 1.0f;
3777}
3778
3779const ImFontGlyph* ImFont::FindGlyph(ImWchar c) const
3780{
3781 if (c >= (size_t)IndexLookup.Size)
3782 return FallbackGlyph;
3783 const ImWchar i = IndexLookup.Data[c];
3784 if (i == (ImWchar)-1)
3785 return FallbackGlyph;
3786 return &Glyphs.Data[i];
3787}
3788
3789const ImFontGlyph* ImFont::FindGlyphNoFallback(ImWchar c) const
3790{
3791 if (c >= (size_t)IndexLookup.Size)
3792 return NULL;
3793 const ImWchar i = IndexLookup.Data[c];
3794 if (i == (ImWchar)-1)
3795 return NULL;
3796 return &Glyphs.Data[i];
3797}
3798
3799// Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
3800static inline const char* CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(const char* text, const char* text_end)
3801{
3802 while (text < text_end && ImCharIsBlankA(*text))
3803 text++;
3804 if (*text == '\n')
3805 text++;
3806 return text;
3807}
3808
3809// Simple word-wrapping for English, not full-featured. Please submit failing cases!
3810// This will return the next location to wrap from. If no wrapping if necessary, this will fast-forward to e.g. text_end.
3811// FIXME: Much possible improvements (don't cut things like "word !", "word!!!" but cut within "word,,,,", more sensible support for punctuations, support for Unicode punctuations, etc.)
3812const char* ImFont::CalcWordWrapPositionA(float scale, const char* text, const char* text_end, float wrap_width) const
3813{
3814 // For references, possible wrap point marked with ^
3815 // "aaa bbb, ccc,ddd. eee fff. ggg!"
3816 // ^ ^ ^ ^ ^__ ^ ^
3817
3818 // List of hardcoded separators: .,;!?'"
3819
3820 // Skip extra blanks after a line returns (that includes not counting them in width computation)
3821 // e.g. "Hello world" --> "Hello" "World"
3822
3823 // Cut words that cannot possibly fit within one line.
3824 // e.g.: "The tropical fish" with ~5 characters worth of width --> "The tr" "opical" "fish"
3825 float line_width = 0.0f;
3826 float word_width = 0.0f;
3827 float blank_width = 0.0f;
3828 wrap_width /= scale; // We work with unscaled widths to avoid scaling every characters
3829
3830 const char* word_end = text;
3831 const char* prev_word_end = NULL;
3832 bool inside_word = true;
3833
3834 const char* s = text;
3835 IM_ASSERT(text_end != NULL);
3836 while (s < text_end)
3837 {
3838 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
3839 const char* next_s;
3840 if (c < 0x80)
3841 next_s = s + 1;
3842 else
3843 next_s = s + ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
3844
3845 if (c < 32)
3846 {
3847 if (c == '\n')
3848 {
3849 line_width = word_width = blank_width = 0.0f;
3850 inside_word = true;
3851 s = next_s;
3852 continue;
3853 }
3854 if (c == '\r')
3855 {
3856 s = next_s;
3857 continue;
3858 }
3859 }
3860
3861 const float char_width = ((int)c < IndexAdvanceX.Size ? IndexAdvanceX.Data[c] : FallbackAdvanceX);
3862 if (ImCharIsBlankW(c))
3863 {
3864 if (inside_word)
3865 {
3866 line_width += blank_width;
3867 blank_width = 0.0f;
3868 word_end = s;
3869 }
3870 blank_width += char_width;
3871 inside_word = false;
3872 }
3873 else
3874 {
3875 word_width += char_width;
3876 if (inside_word)
3877 {
3878 word_end = next_s;
3879 }
3880 else
3881 {
3882 prev_word_end = word_end;
3883 line_width += word_width + blank_width;
3884 word_width = blank_width = 0.0f;
3885 }
3886
3887 // Allow wrapping after punctuation.
3888 inside_word = (c != '.' && c != ',' && c != ';' && c != '!' && c != '?' && c != '\"');
3889 }
3890
3891 // We ignore blank width at the end of the line (they can be skipped)
3892 if (line_width + word_width > wrap_width)
3893 {
3894 // Words that cannot possibly fit within an entire line will be cut anywhere.
3895 if (word_width < wrap_width)
3896 s = prev_word_end ? prev_word_end : word_end;
3897 break;
3898 }
3899
3900 s = next_s;
3901 }
3902
3903 // Wrap_width is too small to fit anything. Force displaying 1 character to minimize the height discontinuity.
3904 // +1 may not be a character start point in UTF-8 but it's ok because caller loops use (text >= word_wrap_eol).
3905 if (s == text && text < text_end)
3906 return s + 1;
3907 return s;
3908}
3909
3910ImVec2 ImFont::CalcTextSizeA(float size, float max_width, float wrap_width, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end, const char** remaining) const
3911{
3912 if (!text_end)
3913 text_end = text_begin + strlen(text_begin); // FIXME-OPT: Need to avoid this.
3914
3915 const float line_height = size;
3916 const float scale = size / FontSize;
3917
3918 ImVec2 text_size = ImVec2(0, 0);
3919 float line_width = 0.0f;
3920
3921 const bool word_wrap_enabled = (wrap_width > 0.0f);
3922 const char* word_wrap_eol = NULL;
3923
3924 const char* s = text_begin;
3925 while (s < text_end)
3926 {
3927 if (word_wrap_enabled)
3928 {
3929 // Calculate how far we can render. Requires two passes on the string data but keeps the code simple and not intrusive for what's essentially an uncommon feature.
3930 if (!word_wrap_eol)
3931 word_wrap_eol = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, text_end, wrap_width - line_width);
3932
3933 if (s >= word_wrap_eol)
3934 {
3935 if (text_size.x < line_width)
3936 text_size.x = line_width;
3937 text_size.y += line_height;
3938 line_width = 0.0f;
3939 word_wrap_eol = NULL;
3940 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end); // Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
3941 continue;
3942 }
3943 }
3944
3945 // Decode and advance source
3946 const char* prev_s = s;
3947 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
3948 if (c < 0x80)
3949 s += 1;
3950 else
3951 s += ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
3952
3953 if (c < 32)
3954 {
3955 if (c == '\n')
3956 {
3957 text_size.x = ImMax(text_size.x, line_width);
3958 text_size.y += line_height;
3959 line_width = 0.0f;
3960 continue;
3961 }
3962 if (c == '\r')
3963 continue;
3964 }
3965
3966 const float char_width = ((int)c < IndexAdvanceX.Size ? IndexAdvanceX.Data[c] : FallbackAdvanceX) * scale;
3967 if (line_width + char_width >= max_width)
3968 {
3969 s = prev_s;
3970 break;
3971 }
3972
3973 line_width += char_width;
3974 }
3975
3976 if (text_size.x < line_width)
3977 text_size.x = line_width;
3978
3979 if (line_width > 0 || text_size.y == 0.0f)
3980 text_size.y += line_height;
3981
3982 if (remaining)
3983 *remaining = s;
3984
3985 return text_size;
3986}
3987
3988// Note: as with every ImDrawList drawing function, this expects that the font atlas texture is bound.
3989void ImFont::RenderChar(ImDrawList* draw_list, float size, const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, ImWchar c) const
3990{
3991 const ImFontGlyph* glyph = FindGlyph(c);
3992 if (!glyph || !glyph->Visible)
3993 return;
3994 if (glyph->Colored)
3995 col |= ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
3996 float scale = (size >= 0.0f) ? (size / FontSize) : 1.0f;
3997 float x = IM_TRUNC(pos.x);
3998 float y = IM_TRUNC(pos.y);
3999 draw_list->PrimReserve(6, 4);
4000 draw_list->PrimRectUV(ImVec2(x + glyph->X0 * scale, y + glyph->Y0 * scale), ImVec2(x + glyph->X1 * scale, y + glyph->Y1 * scale), ImVec2(glyph->U0, glyph->V0), ImVec2(glyph->U1, glyph->V1), col);
4001}
4002
4003// Note: as with every ImDrawList drawing function, this expects that the font atlas texture is bound.
4004void ImFont::RenderText(ImDrawList* draw_list, float size, const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, const ImVec4& clip_rect, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end, float wrap_width, bool cpu_fine_clip) const
4005{
4006 if (!text_end)
4007 text_end = text_begin + strlen(text_begin); // ImGui:: functions generally already provides a valid text_end, so this is merely to handle direct calls.
4008
4009 // Align to be pixel perfect
4010 float x = IM_TRUNC(pos.x);
4011 float y = IM_TRUNC(pos.y);
4012 if (y > clip_rect.w)
4013 return;
4014
4015 const float start_x = x;
4016 const float scale = size / FontSize;
4017 const float line_height = FontSize * scale;
4018 const bool word_wrap_enabled = (wrap_width > 0.0f);
4019
4020 // Fast-forward to first visible line
4021 const char* s = text_begin;
4022 if (y + line_height < clip_rect.y)
4023 while (y + line_height < clip_rect.y && s < text_end)
4024 {
4025 const char* line_end = (const char*)memchr(s, '\n', text_end - s);
4026 if (word_wrap_enabled)
4027 {
4028 // FIXME-OPT: This is not optimal as do first do a search for \n before calling CalcWordWrapPositionA().
4029 // If the specs for CalcWordWrapPositionA() were reworked to optionally return on \n we could combine both.
4030 // However it is still better than nothing performing the fast-forward!
4031 s = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, line_end ? line_end : text_end, wrap_width);
4032 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end);
4033 }
4034 else
4035 {
4036 s = line_end ? line_end + 1 : text_end;
4037 }
4038 y += line_height;
4039 }
4040
4041 // For large text, scan for the last visible line in order to avoid over-reserving in the call to PrimReserve()
4042 // Note that very large horizontal line will still be affected by the issue (e.g. a one megabyte string buffer without a newline will likely crash atm)
4043 if (text_end - s > 10000 && !word_wrap_enabled)
4044 {
4045 const char* s_end = s;
4046 float y_end = y;
4047 while (y_end < clip_rect.w && s_end < text_end)
4048 {
4049 s_end = (const char*)memchr(s_end, '\n', text_end - s_end);
4050 s_end = s_end ? s_end + 1 : text_end;
4051 y_end += line_height;
4052 }
4053 text_end = s_end;
4054 }
4055 if (s == text_end)
4056 return;
4057
4058 // Reserve vertices for remaining worse case (over-reserving is useful and easily amortized)
4059 const int vtx_count_max = (int)(text_end - s) * 4;
4060 const int idx_count_max = (int)(text_end - s) * 6;
4061 const int idx_expected_size = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size + idx_count_max;
4062 draw_list->PrimReserve(idx_count_max, vtx_count_max);
4063 ImDrawVert* vtx_write = draw_list->_VtxWritePtr;
4064 ImDrawIdx* idx_write = draw_list->_IdxWritePtr;
4065 unsigned int vtx_index = draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx;
4066
4067 const ImU32 col_untinted = col | ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
4068 const char* word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4069
4070 while (s < text_end)
4071 {
4072 if (word_wrap_enabled)
4073 {
4074 // Calculate how far we can render. Requires two passes on the string data but keeps the code simple and not intrusive for what's essentially an uncommon feature.
4075 if (!word_wrap_eol)
4076 word_wrap_eol = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, text_end, wrap_width - (x - start_x));
4077
4078 if (s >= word_wrap_eol)
4079 {
4080 x = start_x;
4081 y += line_height;
4082 word_wrap_eol = NULL;
4083 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end); // Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
4084 continue;
4085 }
4086 }
4087
4088 // Decode and advance source
4089 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
4090 if (c < 0x80)
4091 s += 1;
4092 else
4093 s += ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
4094
4095 if (c < 32)
4096 {
4097 if (c == '\n')
4098 {
4099 x = start_x;
4100 y += line_height;
4101 if (y > clip_rect.w)
4102 break; // break out of main loop
4103 continue;
4104 }
4105 if (c == '\r')
4106 continue;
4107 }
4108
4109 const ImFontGlyph* glyph = FindGlyph((ImWchar)c);
4110 if (glyph == NULL)
4111 continue;
4112
4113 float char_width = glyph->AdvanceX * scale;
4114 if (glyph->Visible)
4115 {
4116 // We don't do a second finer clipping test on the Y axis as we've already skipped anything before clip_rect.y and exit once we pass clip_rect.w
4117 float x1 = x + glyph->X0 * scale;
4118 float x2 = x + glyph->X1 * scale;
4119 float y1 = y + glyph->Y0 * scale;
4120 float y2 = y + glyph->Y1 * scale;
4121 if (x1 <= clip_rect.z && x2 >= clip_rect.x)
4122 {
4123 // Render a character
4124 float u1 = glyph->U0;
4125 float v1 = glyph->V0;
4126 float u2 = glyph->U1;
4127 float v2 = glyph->V1;
4128
4129 // CPU side clipping used to fit text in their frame when the frame is too small. Only does clipping for axis aligned quads.
4130 if (cpu_fine_clip)
4131 {
4132 if (x1 < clip_rect.x)
4133 {
4134 u1 = u1 + (1.0f - (x2 - clip_rect.x) / (x2 - x1)) * (u2 - u1);
4135 x1 = clip_rect.x;
4136 }
4137 if (y1 < clip_rect.y)
4138 {
4139 v1 = v1 + (1.0f - (y2 - clip_rect.y) / (y2 - y1)) * (v2 - v1);
4140 y1 = clip_rect.y;
4141 }
4142 if (x2 > clip_rect.z)
4143 {
4144 u2 = u1 + ((clip_rect.z - x1) / (x2 - x1)) * (u2 - u1);
4145 x2 = clip_rect.z;
4146 }
4147 if (y2 > clip_rect.w)
4148 {
4149 v2 = v1 + ((clip_rect.w - y1) / (y2 - y1)) * (v2 - v1);
4150 y2 = clip_rect.w;
4151 }
4152 if (y1 >= y2)
4153 {
4154 x += char_width;
4155 continue;
4156 }
4157 }
4158
4159 // Support for untinted glyphs
4160 ImU32 glyph_col = glyph->Colored ? col_untinted : col;
4161
4162 // We are NOT calling PrimRectUV() here because non-inlined causes too much overhead in a debug builds. Inlined here:
4163 {
4164 vtx_write[0].pos.x = x1; vtx_write[0].pos.y = y1; vtx_write[0].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[0].uv.x = u1; vtx_write[0].uv.y = v1;
4165 vtx_write[1].pos.x = x2; vtx_write[1].pos.y = y1; vtx_write[1].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[1].uv.x = u2; vtx_write[1].uv.y = v1;
4166 vtx_write[2].pos.x = x2; vtx_write[2].pos.y = y2; vtx_write[2].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[2].uv.x = u2; vtx_write[2].uv.y = v2;
4167 vtx_write[3].pos.x = x1; vtx_write[3].pos.y = y2; vtx_write[3].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[3].uv.x = u1; vtx_write[3].uv.y = v2;
4168 idx_write[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index); idx_write[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 1); idx_write[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 2);
4169 idx_write[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index); idx_write[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 2); idx_write[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 3);
4170 vtx_write += 4;
4171 vtx_index += 4;
4172 idx_write += 6;
4173 }
4174 }
4175 }
4176 x += char_width;
4177 }
4178
4179 // Give back unused vertices (clipped ones, blanks) ~ this is essentially a PrimUnreserve() action.
4180 draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size = (int)(vtx_write - draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data); // Same as calling shrink()
4181 draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size = (int)(idx_write - draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data);
4182 draw_list->CmdBuffer[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1].ElemCount -= (idx_expected_size - draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
4183 draw_list->_VtxWritePtr = vtx_write;
4184 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = idx_write;
4185 draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx = vtx_index;
4186}

4188//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4189// [SECTION] ImGui Internal Render Helpers
4190//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4191// Vaguely redesigned to stop accessing ImGui global state:
4192// - RenderArrow()
4193// - RenderBullet()
4194// - RenderCheckMark()
4195// - RenderArrowPointingAt()
4196// - RenderRectFilledRangeH()
4197// - RenderRectFilledWithHole()
4198//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4199// Function in need of a redesign (legacy mess)
4200// - RenderColorRectWithAlphaCheckerboard()
4201//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4202
4203// Render an arrow aimed to be aligned with text (p_min is a position in the same space text would be positioned). To e.g. denote expanded/collapsed state
4204void ImGui::RenderArrow(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col, ImGuiDir dir, float scale)
4205{
4206 const float h = draw_list->_Data->FontSize * 1.00f;
4207 float r = h * 0.40f * scale;
4208 ImVec2 center = pos + ImVec2(h * 0.50f, h * 0.50f * scale);
4209
4210 ImVec2 a, b, c;
4211 switch (dir)
4212 {
4213 case ImGuiDir_Up:
4214 case ImGuiDir_Down:
4215 if (dir == ImGuiDir_Up) r = -r;
4216 a = ImVec2(+0.000f, +0.750f) * r;
4217 b = ImVec2(-0.866f, -0.750f) * r;
4218 c = ImVec2(+0.866f, -0.750f) * r;
4219 break;
4220 case ImGuiDir_Left:
4221 case ImGuiDir_Right:
4222 if (dir == ImGuiDir_Left) r = -r;
4223 a = ImVec2(+0.750f, +0.000f) * r;
4224 b = ImVec2(-0.750f, +0.866f) * r;
4225 c = ImVec2(-0.750f, -0.866f) * r;
4226 break;
4227 case ImGuiDir_None:
4228 case ImGuiDir_COUNT:
4229 IM_ASSERT(0);
4230 break;
4231 }
4232 draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(center + a, center + b, center + c, col);
4233}
4234
4235void ImGui::RenderBullet(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col)
4236{
4237 // FIXME-OPT: This should be baked in font.
4238 draw_list->AddCircleFilled(pos, draw_list->_Data->FontSize * 0.20f, col, 8);
4239}
4240
4241void ImGui::RenderCheckMark(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col, float sz)
4242{
4243 float thickness = ImMax(sz / 5.0f, 1.0f);
4244 sz -= thickness * 0.5f;
4245 pos += ImVec2(thickness * 0.25f, thickness * 0.25f);
4246
4247 float third = sz / 3.0f;
4248 float bx = pos.x + third;
4249 float by = pos.y + sz - third * 0.5f;
4250 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx - third, by - third));
4251 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx, by));
4252 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx + third * 2.0f, by - third * 2.0f));
4253 draw_list->PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
4254}

4256// Render an arrow. 'pos' is position of the arrow tip. half_sz.x is length from base to tip. half_sz.y is length on each side.
4257void ImGui::RenderArrowPointingAt(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImVec2 half_sz, ImGuiDir direction, ImU32 col)
4258{
4259 switch (direction)
4260 {
4261 case ImGuiDir_Left: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
4262 case ImGuiDir_Right: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
4263 case ImGuiDir_Up: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
4264 case ImGuiDir_Down: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
4265 case ImGuiDir_None: case ImGuiDir_COUNT: break; // Fix warnings
4266 }
4267}
4268
4269static inline float ImAcos01(float x)
4270{
4271 if (x <= 0.0f) return IM_PI * 0.5f;
4272 if (x >= 1.0f) return 0.0f;
4273 return ImAcos(x);
4274 //return (-0.69813170079773212f * x * x - 0.87266462599716477f) * x + 1.5707963267948966f; // Cheap approximation, may be enough for what we do.
4275}
4276
4277// FIXME: Cleanup and move code to ImDrawList.
4278void ImGui::RenderRectFilledRangeH(ImDrawList* draw_list, const ImRect& rect, ImU32 col, float x_start_norm, float x_end_norm, float rounding)
4279{
4280 if (x_end_norm == x_start_norm)
4281 return;
4282 if (x_start_norm > x_end_norm)
4283 ImSwap(x_start_norm, x_end_norm);
4284
4285 ImVec2 p0 = ImVec2(ImLerp(rect.Min.x, rect.Max.x, x_start_norm), rect.Min.y);
4286 ImVec2 p1 = ImVec2(ImLerp(rect.Min.x, rect.Max.x, x_end_norm), rect.Max.y);
4287 if (rounding == 0.0f)
4288 {
4289 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p0, p1, col, 0.0f);
4290 return;
4291 }
4292
4293 rounding = ImClamp(ImMin((rect.Max.x - rect.Min.x) * 0.5f, (rect.Max.y - rect.Min.y) * 0.5f) - 1.0f, 0.0f, rounding);
4294 const float inv_rounding = 1.0f / rounding;
4295 const float arc0_b = ImAcos01(1.0f - (p0.x - rect.Min.x) * inv_rounding);
4296 const float arc0_e = ImAcos01(1.0f - (p1.x - rect.Min.x) * inv_rounding);
4297 const float half_pi = IM_PI * 0.5f; // We will == compare to this because we know this is the exact value ImAcos01 can return.
4298 const float x0 = ImMax(p0.x, rect.Min.x + rounding);
4299 if (arc0_b == arc0_e)
4300 {
4301 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x0, p1.y));
4302 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x0, p0.y));
4303 }
4304 else if (arc0_b == 0.0f && arc0_e == half_pi)
4305 {
4306 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x0, p1.y - rounding), rounding, 3, 6); // BL
4307 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x0, p0.y + rounding), rounding, 6, 9); // TR
4308 }
4309 else
4310 {
4311 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x0, p1.y - rounding), rounding, IM_PI - arc0_e, IM_PI - arc0_b); // BL
4312 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x0, p0.y + rounding), rounding, IM_PI + arc0_b, IM_PI + arc0_e); // TR
4313 }
4314 if (p1.x > rect.Min.x + rounding)
4315 {
4316 const float arc1_b = ImAcos01(1.0f - (rect.Max.x - p1.x) * inv_rounding);
4317 const float arc1_e = ImAcos01(1.0f - (rect.Max.x - p0.x) * inv_rounding);
4318 const float x1 = ImMin(p1.x, rect.Max.x - rounding);
4319 if (arc1_b == arc1_e)
4320 {
4321 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x1, p0.y));
4322 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x1, p1.y));
4323 }
4324 else if (arc1_b == 0.0f && arc1_e == half_pi)
4325 {
4326 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x1, p0.y + rounding), rounding, 9, 12); // TR
4327 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x1, p1.y - rounding), rounding, 0, 3); // BR
4328 }
4329 else
4330 {
4331 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x1, p0.y + rounding), rounding, -arc1_e, -arc1_b); // TR
4332 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x1, p1.y - rounding), rounding, +arc1_b, +arc1_e); // BR
4333 }
4334 }
4335 draw_list->PathFillConvex(col);
4336}
4337
4338void ImGui::RenderRectFilledWithHole(ImDrawList* draw_list, const ImRect& outer, const ImRect& inner, ImU32 col, float rounding)
4339{
4340 const bool fill_L = (inner.Min.x > outer.Min.x);
4341 const bool fill_R = (inner.Max.x < outer.Max.x);
4342 const bool fill_U = (inner.Min.y > outer.Min.y);
4343 const bool fill_D = (inner.Max.y < outer.Max.y);
4344 if (fill_L) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, inner.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_U ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) | (fill_D ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft));
4345 if (fill_R) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Min.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, inner.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_U ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight) | (fill_D ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight));
4346 if (fill_U) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Min.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_L ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) | (fill_R ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight));
4347 if (fill_D) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(inner.Max.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_L ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft) | (fill_R ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight));
4348 if (fill_L && fill_U) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft);
4349 if (fill_R && fill_U) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight);
4350 if (fill_L && fill_D) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft);
4351 if (fill_R && fill_D) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight);
4352}
4353
4354// Helper for ColorPicker4()
4355// NB: This is rather brittle and will show artifact when rounding this enabled if rounded corners overlap multiple cells. Caller currently responsible for avoiding that.
4356// Spent a non reasonable amount of time trying to getting this right for ColorButton with rounding+anti-aliasing+ImGuiColorEditFlags_HalfAlphaPreview flag + various grid sizes and offsets, and eventually gave up... probably more reasonable to disable rounding altogether.
4357// FIXME: uses ImGui::GetColorU32
4358void ImGui::RenderColorRectWithAlphaCheckerboard(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 p_min, ImVec2 p_max, ImU32 col, float grid_step, ImVec2 grid_off, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
4359{
4360 if ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == 0)
4361 flags = ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersDefault_;
4362 if (((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) >> IM_COL32_A_SHIFT) < 0xFF)
4363 {
4364 ImU32 col_bg1 = GetColorU32(ImAlphaBlendColors(IM_COL32(204, 204, 204, 255), col));
4365 ImU32 col_bg2 = GetColorU32(ImAlphaBlendColors(IM_COL32(128, 128, 128, 255), col));
4366 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min, p_max, col_bg1, rounding, flags);
4367
4368 int yi = 0;
4369 for (float y = p_min.y + grid_off.y; y < p_max.y; y += grid_step, yi++)
4370 {
4371 float y1 = ImClamp(y, p_min.y, p_max.y), y2 = ImMin(y + grid_step, p_max.y);
4372 if (y2 <= y1)
4373 continue;
4374 for (float x = p_min.x + grid_off.x + (yi & 1) * grid_step; x < p_max.x; x += grid_step * 2.0f)
4375 {
4376 float x1 = ImClamp(x, p_min.x, p_max.x), x2 = ImMin(x + grid_step, p_max.x);
4377 if (x2 <= x1)
4378 continue;
4379 ImDrawFlags cell_flags = ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone;
4380 if (y1 <= p_min.y) { if (x1 <= p_min.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft; if (x2 >= p_max.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight; }
4381 if (y2 >= p_max.y) { if (x1 <= p_min.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft; if (x2 >= p_max.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight; }
4382
4383 // Combine flags
4384 cell_flags = (flags == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone || cell_flags == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone : (cell_flags & flags);
4385 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(x1, y1), ImVec2(x2, y2), col_bg2, rounding, cell_flags);
4386 }
4387 }
4388 }
4389 else
4390 {
4391 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min, p_max, col, rounding, flags);
4392 }
4393}
4394
4395//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4396// [SECTION] Decompression code
4397//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4398// Compressed with stb_compress() then converted to a C array and encoded as base85.
4399// Use the program in misc/fonts/binary_to_compressed_c.cpp to create the array from a TTF file.
4400// The purpose of encoding as base85 instead of "0x00,0x01,..." style is only save on _source code_ size.
4401// Decompression from stb.h (public domain) by Sean Barrett https://github.com/nothings/stb/blob/master/stb.h
4402//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
4403
4404static unsigned int stb_decompress_length(const unsigned char *input)
4405{
4406 return (input[8] << 24) + (input[9] << 16) + (input[10] << 8) + input[11];
4407}
4408
4409static unsigned char *stb__barrier_out_e, *stb__barrier_out_b;
4410static const unsigned char *stb__barrier_in_b;
4411static unsigned char *stb__dout;
4412static void stb__match(const unsigned char *data, unsigned int length)
4413{
4414 // INVERSE of memmove... write each byte before copying the next...
4415 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout + length <= stb__barrier_out_e);
4416 if (stb__dout + length > stb__barrier_out_e) { stb__dout += length; return; }
4417 if (data < stb__barrier_out_b) { stb__dout = stb__barrier_out_e+1; return; }
4418 while (length--) *stb__dout++ = *data++;
4419}
4420
4421static void stb__lit(const unsigned char *data, unsigned int length)
4422{
4423 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout + length <= stb__barrier_out_e);
4424 if (stb__dout + length > stb__barrier_out_e) { stb__dout += length; return; }
4425 if (data < stb__barrier_in_b) { stb__dout = stb__barrier_out_e+1; return; }
4426 memcpy(stb__dout, data, length);
4427 stb__dout += length;
4428}
4429
4430#define stb__in2(x) ((i[x] << 8) + i[(x)+1])
4431#define stb__in3(x) ((i[x] << 16) + stb__in2((x)+1))
4432#define stb__in4(x) ((i[x] << 24) + stb__in3((x)+1))
4433
4434static const unsigned char *stb_decompress_token(const unsigned char *i)
4435{
4436 if (*i >= 0x20) { // use fewer if's for cases that expand small
4437 if (*i >= 0x80) stb__match(stb__dout-i[1]-1, i[0] - 0x80 + 1), i += 2;
4438 else if (*i >= 0x40) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in2(0) - 0x4000 + 1), i[2]+1), i += 3;
4439 else /* *i >= 0x20 */ stb__lit(i+1, i[0] - 0x20 + 1), i += 1 + (i[0] - 0x20 + 1);
4440 } else { // more ifs for cases that expand large, since overhead is amortized
4441 if (*i >= 0x18) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(0) - 0x180000 + 1), i[3]+1), i += 4;
4442 else if (*i >= 0x10) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(0) - 0x100000 + 1), stb__in2(3)+1), i += 5;
4443 else if (*i >= 0x08) stb__lit(i+2, stb__in2(0) - 0x0800 + 1), i += 2 + (stb__in2(0) - 0x0800 + 1);
4444 else if (*i == 0x07) stb__lit(i+3, stb__in2(1) + 1), i += 3 + (stb__in2(1) + 1);
4445 else if (*i == 0x06) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(1)+1), i[4]+1), i += 5;
4446 else if (*i == 0x04) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(1)+1), stb__in2(4)+1), i += 6;
4447 }
4448 return i;
4449}
4450
4451static unsigned int stb_adler32(unsigned int adler32, unsigned char *buffer, unsigned int buflen)
4452{
4453 const unsigned long ADLER_MOD = 65521;
4454 unsigned long s1 = adler32 & 0xffff, s2 = adler32 >> 16;
4455 unsigned long blocklen = buflen % 5552;
4456
4457 unsigned long i;
4458 while (buflen) {
4459 for (i=0; i + 7 < blocklen; i += 8) {
4460 s1 += buffer[0], s2 += s1;
4461 s1 += buffer[1], s2 += s1;
4462 s1 += buffer[2], s2 += s1;
4463 s1 += buffer[3], s2 += s1;
4464 s1 += buffer[4], s2 += s1;
4465 s1 += buffer[5], s2 += s1;
4466 s1 += buffer[6], s2 += s1;
4467 s1 += buffer[7], s2 += s1;
4468
4469 buffer += 8;
4470 }
4471
4472 for (; i < blocklen; ++i)
4473 s1 += *buffer++, s2 += s1;
4474
4475 s1 %= ADLER_MOD, s2 %= ADLER_MOD;
4476 buflen -= blocklen;
4477 blocklen = 5552;
4478 }
4479 return (unsigned int)(s2 << 16) + (unsigned int)s1;
4480}
4481
4482static unsigned int stb_decompress(unsigned char *output, const unsigned char *i, unsigned int /*length*/)
4483{
4484 if (stb__in4(0) != 0x57bC0000) return 0;
4485 if (stb__in4(4) != 0) return 0; // error! stream is > 4GB
4486 const unsigned int olen = stb_decompress_length(i);
4487 stb__barrier_in_b = i;
4488 stb__barrier_out_e = output + olen;
4489 stb__barrier_out_b = output;
4490 i += 16;
4491
4492 stb__dout = output;
4493 for (;;) {
4494 const unsigned char *old_i = i;
4495 i = stb_decompress_token(i);
4496 if (i == old_i) {
4497 if (*i == 0x05 && i[1] == 0xfa) {
4498 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout == output + olen);
4499 if (stb__dout != output + olen) return 0;
4500 if (stb_adler32(1, output, olen) != (unsigned int) stb__in4(2))
4501 return 0;
4502 return olen;
4503 } else {
4504 IM_ASSERT(0); /* NOTREACHED */
4505 return 0;
4506 }
4507 }
4508 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout <= output + olen);
4509 if (stb__dout > output + olen)
4510 return 0;
4511 }
4512}
